RAS: Measuring LLM Safety Through Refusal Alignment
Authors: Chang-Chieh Huang, Yan-Lun Chen, Chia-Mu Yu, Wei-Bin Lee
First: 2026-06-24T12:19:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-24T12:19:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) is commonly performed by querying models with unsafe or jailbreak prompts and judging whether their outputs violate a safety policy. Although useful, output-level evaluation is expensive, sensitive to judge choice, and easily tied to fixed question banks. We propose **SafeVec**, a white-box evaluation procedure that measures safety from internal representations rather than generated answers. **SafeVec** first extracts layer-wise refusal directions from a safety-aligned reference model, then selects stable layer windows where safe and unsafe behaviors are separable, and finally scores a target model by measuring whether its hidden states align with these refusal directions under unsafe and jailbreak prompts. The resulting metric, **RAS** (**R**efusal **A**lignment **S**core), maps representation-level refusal alignment to a calibrated 0-100 safety score. Across `Llama`, `Gemma`, and `Qwen` model families, RAS separates aligned models from uncensored and abliterated variants, tracks output-level attack success rate, and is substantially faster than judge-based evaluation. These results suggest that refusal alignment provides a compact and efficient signal for white-box LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RAS：通过拒绝对齐测量大型语言模型的安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全性评估通常通过使用不安全或越狱提示查询模型，并判断其输出是否违反安全政策。尽管有用，输出级评估成本高、对评判者选择敏感，并且容易与固定问题库挂钩。我们提出了**SafeVec**，一种白盒评估程序，通过内部表示而非生成答案来测量安全性。**SafeVec**首先从安全对齐的参考模型中提取逐层拒绝方向，然后选择安全和不安全行为可分离的稳定层窗口，最后通过测量目标模型的隐藏状态在不安全和越狱提示下是否与这些拒绝方向对齐来评分。最终指标**RAS**（**R**efusal **A**lignment **S**core）将表示级拒绝对齐映射到校准的0-100安全分数。在`Llama`、`Gemma`和`Qwen`模型系列中，RAS将对齐模型与未审查和被消除的变体区分开，跟踪输出级攻击成功率，并且比基于评判者的评估快得多。这些结果表明，拒绝对齐为白盒LLM安全评估提供了紧凑而高效的信号。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of evaluating the safety of large language models (LLMs), which has traditionally relied on output-level assessments that are costly, subjective, and dependent on fixed question banks. Existing methods often struggle with these limitations, prompting the authors to propose a novel approach called SafeVec, which evaluates safety through internal representations rather than generated outputs. This method is well-motivated as it aims to provide a more efficient and reliable safety metric. The paper introduces the Refusal Alignment Score (RAS), derived from extracting layer-wise refusal directions from a safety-aligned reference model and measuring alignment of hidden states in target models. The methodology demonstrates that RAS effectively distinguishes between aligned and uncensored models across various model families, showing a strong correlation with output-level attack success rates while being significantly faster than traditional judge-based evaluations, thus supporting the goal of improving LLM safety assessment.
本研究旨在有效评估大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全性，传统方法通常依赖于输出级评估，这种方法成本高且容易受到主观判断的影响。以往的方法往往依赖固定的问题库，且在不同模型间的泛化能力有限。所提出的方法SafeVec通过评估内部表示而非生成的输出来创新性地评估安全性，从而克服了现有方法的局限性。SafeVec从安全对齐的参考模型中提取逐层拒绝方向，并根据目标模型的隐藏状态与这些方向在不安全提示下的对齐程度进行评分。本文的贡献在于引入拒绝对齐评分（RAS），该评分提供了一种有效区分对齐模型和未审查模型的校准安全指标，显示出在评估速度和可靠性方面相较于传统方法的显著提升。
FinRED: An Expert-Guided Benchmark Generation and Evaluation Framework for Financial LLM Red-Teaming
Authors: Chaeyun Kim, Daeyoung Park, Junghwan Kim, Jinyoung Jeong, Eunji Song, Yongtaek Lim, Minwoo Kim
First: 2026-06-18T07:46:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-24T07:42:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Existing safety benchmarks target general adversarial scenarios but miss finance-specific risks. Financial LLMs face regulatory compliance violations, fraud facilitation, and systemic trust erosion that require targeted evaluation. We introduce FinRED, an expert-guided red-teaming framework for financial LLM safety evaluation developed with financial experts. FinRED uses a novel two-level taxonomy mapping global standards (e.g., FATF and EU DORA) to threats ranging from regulatory evasion to complex fraud, integrated with a scalable pipeline that converts real financial documents into context-rich red-teaming Behavioral Prompts (seeds) through an expert-defined schema. Rigorous expert validation confirms seed plausibility and realism for meaningful LLM safety evaluation. We also provide an expert-validated, finance-specific rubric that goes beyond disclaimer checks, aligns more closely with human experts than static one-size-fits-all rubrics, and reduces critical false negatives from 28 to 12. Aligned with internationally adopted risk-management and information-security standards (e.g., ISO/IEC 27001), FinRED is deployed in South Korea's Financial Security Institute (FSI) regulatory sandbox for generative AI security evaluation in real financial services. To mitigate dual-use risks, the dataset, generation pipeline, prompt template, and evaluation framework are gated for qualified researchers at https://github.com/selectstar-ai/FinRED-paper and https://huggingface.co/datasets/datumo/FinRED.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FinRED：一个专家指导的金融LLM红队评估基准生成框架
现有的安全基准针对一般对抗场景，但忽视了金融特定风险。金融LLM面临合规性违规、欺诈促进和系统性信任侵蚀等问题，需要针对性评估。我们推出了FinRED，这是一个由金融专家开发的专家指导的金融LLM安全评估红队框架。FinRED使用一种新颖的两级分类法，将全球标准（如FATF和EU DORA）映射到从监管规避到复杂欺诈的威胁，结合一个可扩展的管道，通过专家定义的模式将真实金融文档转换为上下文丰富的红队行为提示（种子）。严格的专家验证确认了种子的合理性和真实性，以便进行有意义的LLM安全评估。我们还提供了一个经过专家验证的金融特定评分标准，超越了免责声明检查，更加贴近人类专家，而不是静态的一刀切评分标准，并将关键的假阴性从28减少到12。FinRED与国际公认的风险管理和信息安全标准（如ISO/IEC 27001）保持一致，已在韩国金融安全研究所（FSI）的监管沙箱中部署，用于真实金融服务中的生成AI安全评估。为了减轻双重用途风险，数据集、生成管道、提示模板和评估框架对合格研究人员进行了限制，网址为https://github.com/selectstar-ai/FinRED-paper和https://huggingface.co/datasets/datumo/FinRED。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacy of existing safety benchmarks for financial large language models (LLMs), which often overlook finance-specific risks such as regulatory compliance violations and fraud. Previous methods primarily focused on general adversarial scenarios and lacked targeted evaluation frameworks, leading to critical gaps in assessing financial LLM safety. The proposed FinRED framework, developed with financial experts, introduces a two-level taxonomy that maps global standards to specific threats and utilizes a scalable pipeline to generate context-rich red-teaming Behavioral Prompts from real financial documents. This approach is well-motivated as it aims to enhance the evaluation of financial LLMs by providing a finance-specific rubric that significantly reduces false negatives. The methodology includes expert validation of prompts and a deployment in South Korea's Financial Security Institute regulatory sandbox, achieving a reduction in critical false negatives from 28 to 12, thereby supporting the goal of improving safety evaluations in financial services.
本研究解决了现有金融大型语言模型（LLM）安全基准的不足，这些基准主要关注一般对抗场景，而忽视了金融特定风险，如合规违规和欺诈。以往的方法缺乏针对性，通常导致较高的假阴性率。提出的FinRED框架在金融专家的指导下开发，引入了一个两级分类法，将全球标准与特定金融威胁对齐，并利用可扩展的管道从真实金融文档中创建上下文丰富的红队行为提示。该专家指导的方法不仅增强了评估种子的现实性和可信度，还显著降低了假阴性率，从28降至12，从而改善了金融LLM的安全评估。FinRED已在韩国金融安全研究所的监管沙箱中实施，证明其在真实金融服务安全评估中的有效性。
How Reliable Is Your Jailbreak Judge? Calibration and Adversarial Robustness of Automated ASR Scoring
Authors: Yang Gao
First: 2026-06-24T07:14:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-24T07:14:17+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 3 figures, 2 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Almost every paper on LLM jailbreaks and prompt injection reports an attack-success rate (ASR), and that number is assigned not by people but by an automated judge: either a safety classifier trained for the task, or a general chat model prompted to grade. The judge is rarely checked. We check it. Using 596 human-labeled completions from the HarmBench classifier validation set, we compare the two judge families against human majority votes and then attack them. The two families fail in opposite ways. The dedicated classifier over-flags (precision 0.835, recall 0.974); three different LLM-as-judges keep high precision (0.81 to 0.94) but show erratic recall (0.06 to 0.65), so the same responses produce very different ASR depending on which judge scores them. The two families also differ sharply in robustness. Wrappers that leave the harmful text untouched and only add benign framing flip every LLM-judge between 57% and 100% of the time, and a single prepended refusal sentence accounts for much of this (39% to 88%). The dedicated classifier resists these surface attacks (at most 6.7%), but a white-box GCG attack on its open weights flips 70% of confident true positives (21 of 30; 95% CI 54 to 86%) even at a small optimization budget. A two-annotator audit confirms the attacks leave the harm intact: every one of 80 sampled flips still contained the harmful content. Because a large and growing share of reported ASR comes from LLM-judges, many such numbers are unreliable both on average and under deliberate pressure. We recommend that papers report judge precision and recall on a human-labeled slice, report ASR corrected for judge precision, and include an adversarial check of the judge. Our code is released.
中文标题/摘要
标题：你的越狱评估器有多可靠？自动化ASR评分的校准与对抗鲁棒性
几乎每篇关于LLM越狱和提示注入的论文都报告了攻击成功率（ASR），而这个数字不是由人类赋予的，而是由一个自动评估器给出的：要么是为此任务训练的安全分类器，要么是被提示进行评分的一般聊天模型。评估器很少被检查。我们进行了检查。使用来自HarmBench分类器验证集的596个人工标注的完成结果，我们将这两种评估器与人类多数投票进行比较，然后对其进行攻击。这两种评估器在失败方式上截然相反。专用分类器过度标记（精确度0.835，召回率0.974）；三种不同的LLM作为评估者保持高精度（0.81到0.94），但显示出不稳定的召回率（0.06到0.65），因此相同的响应根据哪个评估者评分会产生非常不同的ASR。这两种评估器在鲁棒性上也有显著差异。那些不改变有害文本，仅添加良性框架的包装器使每个LLM评估者在57%到100%的时间内翻转，而一个单独的前置拒绝句子占据了其中很大一部分（39%到88%）。专用分类器抵御这些表面攻击（最多6.7%），但对其开放权重的白盒GCG攻击在小的优化预算下翻转了70%的自信真阳性（30个中的21个；95%置信区间54到86%）。两位标注者的审计确认攻击保持了有害内容的完整性：80个抽样翻转中的每一个仍然包含有害内容。由于越来越多的报告ASR来自LLM评估者，许多这样的数字在平均值和故意压力下都是不可靠的。我们建议论文报告人类标注样本上的评估器精度和召回率，报告经过评估器精度修正的ASR，并包括对评估器的对抗性检查。我们的代码已发布。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the reliability of automated judges used in evaluating attack-success rates (ASR) for LLM jailbreaks and prompt injections, highlighting that these judges are seldom validated against human assessments. Previous methods relied on either dedicated safety classifiers or general chat models, which exhibited significant flaws: the classifiers tended to over-flag harmful content while LLM judges showed inconsistent recall rates. The proposed approach involves a comprehensive evaluation of these judges against human majority votes and subsequent adversarial attacks, revealing that while dedicated classifiers maintain robustness, LLM judges are easily manipulated. The paper contributes by demonstrating the unreliability of current ASR metrics and recommending improved reporting standards for judge performance. The methodology includes a comparison of human-labeled completions and adversarial testing, achieving insights that indicate many reported ASR figures may be misleading, thus supporting the need for more rigorous validation processes.
本研究关注用于评估大型语言模型（LLM）越狱和提示注入攻击成功率（ASR）的自动评判者的可靠性，强调这些评判者缺乏验证。以往的方法依赖于专用的安全分类器或通用聊天模型，但这两者在精确度和召回率上均存在显著缺陷，导致ASR结果不一致。所提出的方法涉及对这些评判者进行系统评估，使用人工标注的数据，揭示专用分类器倾向于过度标记，而LLM评判者的召回率则表现不稳定。该研究的贡献在于展示了这些评判者对对抗性攻击的脆弱性，并建议未来研究报告评判者的性能指标并包含对抗性检查。研究方法包括使用验证集比较评判者的性能，并分析它们对各种攻击的鲁棒性，最终表明许多报告的ASR数据可能不可靠，从而支持改进评估标准的必要性。
TROPT: An Open Framework for Unifying and Advancing Discrete Text Optimization
Authors: Matan Ben-Tov, Mahmood Sharif
First: 2026-06-22T15:44:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-22T15:44:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Discrete text-trigger optimization -- searching for text sequences that, when ingested by a model, steer it toward a specified objective -- underpins model red-teaming (e.g., LLM jailbreaks), as well as auditing and interpretability. However, the current state of discrete optimizers hinders their adoption and progress. First, existing optimizers, when open-sourced at all, are scattered across research codebases tied to specific models, objectives, and problem domains. Second, optimizer variants proliferate, each requiring engineering overhead to use or extend, and remaining hard to compare head-to-head. Together, these raise the bar for adopting optimizers in existing or new domains, and for advancing them via new strategies. We address these gaps with TROPT, the first open-source framework that unifies discrete optimizers' execution and standardizes their development under a single interface. TROPT makes it easy to customize end-to-end optimization recipes by swapping any component -- models, objectives, and optimizers -- extending its reach across domains and new applications. TROPT currently ships with 30+ optimization recipes -- covering applications such as jailbreaking and probing model internals -- built from 15+ optimizers (spanning white-box to black-box access) and 15+ losses, from foundational to state-of-the-art methods. Demonstrating its utility, we leverage TROPT in several studies: (i) controlled, large-scale experiments comparing and enhancing optimization strategies for LLM jailbreaks, revealing potent-yet-underadopted techniques; and (ii) porting optimizers from one domain (e.g., LLM jailbreak) to new domains (e.g., corpus-poisoning embedding model). In all, TROPT significantly lowers the barrier to adopting and advancing discrete text optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TROPT：统一和推进离散文本优化的开放框架
离散文本触发优化——寻找文本序列，当被模型摄取时，引导其朝向特定目标——是模型红队（例如，LLM越狱）以及审计和可解释性的基础。然而，当前离散优化器的状态阻碍了它们的采用和进展。首先，现有的优化器，即使开源，也分散在与特定模型、目标和问题领域相关的研究代码库中。其次，优化器变体层出不穷，每个都需要工程开销来使用或扩展，并且难以进行直接比较。这些因素共同提高了在现有或新领域中采用优化器的门槛，并通过新策略推进它们。我们通过TROPT解决这些问题，这是第一个统一离散优化器执行并在单一接口下标准化其开发的开源框架。TROPT使得通过更换任何组件——模型、目标和优化器——轻松定制端到端优化配方，扩展其在各个领域和新应用中的覆盖范围。TROPT目前提供30多个优化配方——涵盖越狱和探测模型内部等应用——由15个以上的优化器（从白盒到黑盒访问）和15个以上的损失函数（从基础到最先进的方法）构建。为了展示其效用，我们在几项研究中利用TROPT：（i）控制的大规模实验比较和增强LLM越狱的优化策略，揭示出强大但未被广泛采用的技术；（ii）将优化器从一个领域（例如，LLM越狱）移植到新领域（例如，语料库中毒嵌入模型）。总之，TROPT显著降低了采用和推进离散文本优化的门槛。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenges in discrete text-trigger optimization, which is crucial for tasks like model red-teaming and interpretability, highlighting that existing optimizers are often fragmented, model-specific, and difficult to compare. Previous methods have led to inefficiencies due to their scattered nature and the engineering overhead required for their use, prompting the need for a unified approach. The paper introduces TROPT, an open-source framework that standardizes the execution and development of discrete optimizers, allowing for easy customization and extension across various applications. TROPT includes over 30 optimization recipes and supports more than 15 optimizers and losses, demonstrating its effectiveness through large-scale experiments that enhance optimization strategies for tasks like LLM jailbreaks and enable the transfer of optimizers across different domains. The results indicate that TROPT significantly facilitates the adoption and advancement of discrete text optimization techniques.
本研究解决了离散文本触发优化中的挑战，这对于模型红队和可解释性等任务至关重要。以往的方法往往是分散的，依赖于特定的模型和目标，导致其难以采用和比较。所提出的方法TROPT是一个开源框架，统一了离散优化器，提供了单一接口，便于在各种应用中进行定制和扩展。该框架包含超过30个优化配方，整合了15种以上的优化器和损失函数，促进了现有策略的增强和新领域的探索。该方法通过大规模实验验证了其有效性，改善了LLM越狱等任务的优化策略，并展示了优化器在不同领域之间的可迁移性，有效降低了离散文本优化的采用和进步的门槛。
Culturally-Adapted Red-Teaming Across East and Southeast Asian Contexts: A Methodological and Comparative Analysis
Authors: Hyeji Choi, Yongtaek Lim, Minwoo Kim
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-06-08T08:17:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-22T07:46:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICML 2026 Workshop on Culture X AI
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multilingual safety evaluation of large language models (LLMs) has predominantly relied on direct translation (DT) of English benchmarks into target languages - an approach that converts surface-level linguistic form while failing to reflect the cultural context embedded in threat scenarios, social norms, and legal frameworks. We construct paired DT and culturally-adapted (CA) datasets via 1:1 seed matching for four languages - Korean (KO), Japanese (JA), Thai (TH), and Khmer (KM) - and compare Attack Success Rate (ASR) and Cultural Realism scores across four open-source LLM. CA prompts yield Delta-ASR > 0 across all 16 language x model combinations (mean +9.3 pp), and DT-based evaluation underestimates risk in 44 of 48 category x language combinations. Language-level analysis reveals that the distribution of threat forms is heterogeneous across languages. Cultural Realism analysis further shows that DT Cultural Depth (C3) scores remain consistently below 1.0 out of 3.0 across all four languages (mean 0.17), whereas CA scores reach up to 2.51, indicating that direct translation produces inputs systematically divergent from those encountered in real-world multicultural settings. These findings demonstrate that adapting benchmarks to language-specific cultural contexts - rather than relying on linguistic translation alone - is necessary for valid multilingual LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：跨东亚和东南亚背景的文化适应性红队：方法论和比较分析
大型语言模型（LLMs）的多语言安全评估主要依赖于将英语基准直接翻译（DT）为目标语言，这种方法仅转换表层语言形式，未能反映威胁场景、社会规范和法律框架中嵌入的文化背景。我们通过1:1种子匹配构建了四种语言（韩语、日语、泰语和高棉语）的配对DT和文化适应（CA）数据集，并比较了四个开源LLM的攻击成功率（ASR）和文化现实评分。CA提示在所有16种语言x模型组合中均产生Delta-ASR > 0（平均+9.3个百分点），而基于DT的评估在48个类别x语言组合中低估了风险。语言级分析显示，威胁形式的分布在不同语言中是异质的。文化现实分析进一步表明，DT文化深度（C3）评分在所有四种语言中始终低于3.0的1.0（平均0.17），而CA评分高达2.51，表明直接翻译产生的输入与现实世界多文化环境中遇到的输入系统性地不同。这些发现表明，适应特定语言文化背景的基准是有效的多语言LLM安全评估所必需的，而不仅仅依赖语言翻译。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of multilingual safety evaluations of large language models (LLMs), which have primarily depended on direct translation (DT) of English benchmarks, failing to account for cultural contexts. Previous methods have overlooked the nuances of social norms and legal frameworks, leading to an underestimation of risks in non-English languages. This paper proposes a culturally-adapted (CA) approach that constructs paired DT and CA datasets for Korean, Japanese, Thai, and Khmer languages, allowing for a more accurate assessment of LLM performance. The methodology involves comparing Attack Success Rate (ASR) and Cultural Realism scores across four open-source LLMs, revealing that CA prompts significantly improve ASR and better reflect cultural depth. The results indicate that adapting benchmarks to specific cultural contexts is essential for effective multilingual LLM safety evaluation, with CA methods achieving a mean Delta-ASR increase of 9.3 percentage points and higher Cultural Realism scores compared to DT methods.
本研究解决了大型语言模型（LLMs）多语言安全评估中的不足之处，传统上依赖于将英语基准直接翻译成其他语言，未能考虑文化背景。以往的方法忽视了文化规范和法律框架的影响，导致在非英语场景中低估了风险。本文提出了一种文化适应（CA）的方法，通过种子匹配构建韩语、日语、泰语和高棉语的配对数据集，从而更准确地评估威胁场景。该方法比较了四个开源LLM的攻击成功率（ASR）和文化现实评分，结果显示，与直接翻译相比，CA提示显著提高了ASR和文化相关性。结果表明，CA方法在ASR上平均提高了9.3个百分点，并强调了文化信息基准在有效的多语言LLM安全评估中的必要性。
AgentLens: Interpretable Safety Steering via Mechanistic Subspaces for Multi-Turn Coding Agent
Authors: Weidi Luo, Qiming Zhang, Yihao Quan, Mingyu Jin, Jie Cai, Chaowei Xiao, Jingcheng Niu, Zhen Xiang
First: 2026-06-21T21:13:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-21T21:13:55+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Coding agents based on large language models (LLMs) demonstrate remarkable autonomous capabilities, but they also introduce significant safety and misuse risks during multi-turn interactions with external environments. Existing safety mechanisms mainly rely on external guardrails, which have a limited ability to perform fine-grained behavioral control during execution. Meanwhile, recent mechanistic interpretability methods for LLM safety are mostly confined to single-turn or jailbreak-style QA settings, limiting their ability to capture the evolving risk dynamics of multi-turn agent execution. In this paper, we investigate the safety of multi-turn coding agents from an internal perspective. We propose AgentLens (Mechanistic Subspace Intervention and Steering), a white-box defense framework that performs runtime safety detection and representation-level mitigation for coding agents. Unlike conventional agent guardrails, AgentLens detect harmful execution states from step-level hidden representations and mitigate unsafe behavior by intervening in a 10-dimensional subspace within a single layer. To support this research, we introduce the Mechanistic Agent Safety (MAS) benchmark, comprising comprehensively annotated multi-turn execution trajectories across 194 tasks using LLaMA-3.1-8B, Qwen-2.5-7B, and Gemma-2-9B. Extensive experiments show that AgentLens achieves strong safety detection performance, provides preliminary evidence for lookahead risk anticipation, and substantially reduces harmful actions of the coding agent, establishing a foundation for applying mechanistic interpretability to dynamic LLM agent safety. The code is available at: https://github.com/EddyLuo1232/AgentLens
中文标题/摘要
标题：AgentLens：通过机制子空间实现可解释的多轮编码代理安全引导
基于大型语言模型（LLMs）的编码代理展示了显著的自主能力，但在与外部环境的多轮交互中也引入了重大安全和误用风险。现有的安全机制主要依赖外部护栏，在执行过程中对细粒度行为控制的能力有限。同时，最近的LLM安全机制可解释性方法大多局限于单轮或越狱式问答设置，限制了其捕捉多轮代理执行中不断变化的风险动态的能力。本文从内部视角研究多轮编码代理的安全性。我们提出了AgentLens（机制子空间干预与引导），这是一个白盒防御框架，能够对编码代理进行运行时安全检测和表示级别的缓解。与传统的代理护栏不同，AgentLens通过从步骤级隐藏表示中检测有害执行状态，并通过干预单层内的10维子空间来缓解不安全行为。为了支持这项研究，我们引入了机制代理安全（MAS）基准，涵盖了使用LLaMA-3.1-8B、Qwen-2.5-7B和Gemma-2-9B的194个任务的全面注释的多轮执行轨迹。大量实验表明，AgentLens实现了强大的安全检测性能，为前瞻性风险预判提供了初步证据，并显著减少了编码代理的有害行为，为将机制可解释性应用于动态LLM代理安全奠定了基础。代码可在：https://github.com/EddyLuo1232/AgentLens

This research addresses the safety risks associated with multi-turn coding agents based on large language models (LLMs), which have shown impressive autonomous capabilities but also pose significant misuse risks. Previous safety mechanisms primarily relied on external guardrails, which lack fine-grained control during execution, and existing interpretability methods were limited to single-turn interactions, failing to capture the evolving risks in multi-turn contexts. The paper contributes by presenting the Mechanistic Agent Safety (MAS) benchmark, which includes annotated multi-turn execution trajectories across 194 tasks, and demonstrates that AgentLens significantly improves safety detection performance and reduces harmful actions, supporting the goal of enhancing LLM agent safety during dynamic interactions.

SPHINX: First Explain, Then Explore
Authors: Nguyen Do, Tue M. Cao, Tien Van Do, András Hajdu, Tamás Bérczes, My T. Thai
First: 2026-06-16T03:48:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-16T03:48:27+00:00
Comments: 13 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generating adversarial driving scenarios is critical for evaluating and improving autonomous vehicle decision-making systems in simulation. Recent approaches, such as ChatScene and LLM-Attacker, rely primarily on the prior knowledge of Large Language Models and Vision-Language Models to generate driving scenarios procedurally. We argue that adversarial scenes should be generated based on the failure diagnosis (e.g., indecisiveness, multi-frame inconsistency) of the driving policy to specifically address the policy's weaknesses instead of relying on prior assumptions. In this paper, we propose SPHINX, a closed-loop framework for adversarial scenario synthesis guided by a simple principle: first explain, then explore. Beyond blindly exploring the scenario space, SPHINX leverages explainable artificial intelligence methods to analyze the policy, identifying key visual concepts and their influence on policy outputs, and the uncertainty of the decisions. Given the interpretable evidence extracted from the policy's own decision process, we use a vision language model to rationalize and criticize failure modes of the current policy. These critics are then used to generate targeted adversarial scenarios for policy retraining and improvement. We demonstrate that SPHINX can highlight an interpretable account of policy failures while other adversarial scene generation cannot. Across the evaluated benchmarks and test suites, SPHINX can be applied to diverse state-of-the-art autonomous vehicle architectures and yields consistent robustness improvements over existing scenario-generation methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPHINX：先解释，再探索
生成对抗驾驶场景对于评估和改进自主车辆决策系统在仿真中的表现至关重要。最近的方法，如ChatScene和LLM-Attacker，主要依赖于大型语言模型和视觉-语言模型的先验知识来程序化生成驾驶场景。我们认为，对抗场景应基于驾驶策略的失败诊断（例如，优柔寡断、多帧不一致）生成，以具体解决策略的弱点，而不是依赖先前假设。本文提出了SPHINX，一个闭环框架，用于对抗场景合成，其指导原则是：先解释，再探索。SPHINX不仅仅是盲目探索场景空间，而是利用可解释人工智能方法分析策略，识别关键视觉概念及其对策略输出的影响，以及决策的不确定性。根据从策略自身决策过程中提取的可解释证据，我们使用视觉语言模型来合理化和批评当前策略的失败模式。这些批评随后用于生成针对性的对抗场景，以进行策略再训练和改进。我们证明SPHINX能够突出政策失败的可解释性，而其他对抗场景生成方法则无法做到。在评估的基准和测试套件中，SPHINX可以应用于多种最先进的自主车辆架构，并在现有场景生成方法上实现一致的鲁棒性提升。

This approach not only rationalizes the failures but also generates targeted adversarial scenarios for retraining, demonstrating that SPHINX provides interpretable insights into policy failures. The methodology shows consistent robustness improvements across various benchmarks and test suites when applied to state-of-the-art autonomous vehicle architectures, supporting the goal of enhancing decision-making systems.

Enhancing LLM Safety Through a Theoretical Minimax Game Lens
Authors: Yihe Deng, Yu Yang, Junkai Zhang, Wei Wang, Bo Li
First: 2025-02-07T18:45:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-15T02:50:15+00:00
Comments: 24 pages, 9 figures, 5 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid advancement of large language models (LLMs) necessitates effective mechanisms to ensure their responsible deployment by accurately distinguishing unsafe content from benign content. While substantial safety datasets are available in English, multilingual safety modeling remains underexplored due to limited open-source safety datasets in other languages. Even within English datasets, safe yet sensitive corner-case content is scarce, leading to shortcut learning by models and non-trivial false-positive rates. To mitigate these issues, we introduce a novel minimax reinforcement learning (RL) framework wherein a data generator and a classifier model co-evolve, facilitating the production of high-quality synthetic multilingual safety data. We theoretically formalize this interaction as a minimax game and rigorously demonstrate convergence to a Nash equilibrium. Empirical evaluations confirm that our synthetic data generation method significantly enhances the classifier model performance, enabling a substantially smaller model to surpass the state-of-the-art by nearly 10% on English benchmarks while achieving 4.5x faster inference speed. These results establish a scalable and efficient methodology for synthetic data generation, advancing the development of safer and more robust multilingual LLM deployments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过理论最小最大博弈视角增强大型语言模型安全性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展需要有效机制，以确保其负责任的部署，准确区分不安全内容与良性内容。虽然英语中有大量安全数据集，但由于其他语言中开放源代码安全数据集有限，多语言安全建模仍未得到充分探索。即使在英语数据集中，安全但敏感的边缘案例内容也很稀缺，导致模型的捷径学习和非平凡的误报率。为了解决这些问题，我们引入了一种新颖的最小最大强化学习（RL）框架，其中数据生成器和分类模型共同进化，促进高质量合成多语言安全数据的生成。我们将这种交互理论化为最小最大博弈，并严格证明收敛到纳什均衡。实证评估确认我们的合成数据生成方法显著提升了分类模型的性能，使得一个显著更小的模型在英语基准测试中超越了最先进的技术近10%，同时实现了4.5倍的推理速度提升。这些结果建立了一种可扩展且高效的合成数据生成方法，推动了更安全、更强大的多语言LLM部署的发展。

This methodology contributes to the field by significantly improving classifier performance, with empirical results showing a nearly 10% improvement over state-of-the-art models on English benchmarks and achieving 4.5 times faster inference speed, thus supporting the goal of safer multilingual LLM deployments.

GAS-Leak-LLM: Genetic Algorithm-Based Suffix Optimization for Black-Box LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Aman Anifer, Vignesh Kumar Kembu, Vishnu M, Antonino Nocera, Vinod P., Amal Murali PK, Akshay S Rajan
First: 2026-06-14T12:41:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-14T12:41:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) constitute pivotal components within the AI-dominated information technology ecosystem. To mitigate risks associated with harmful or policy-violating outputs, commercial systems employ advanced alignment strategies and multi-layered content moderation mechanisms. Despite these safeguards, recent research has demonstrated that LLMs remain vulnerable to adversarial manipulation, particularly through jailbreaking and prompt injection techniques. In this work, we propose GAS-Leak-LLM a novel jailbreaking attack based on a genetic algorithm that systematically evolves adversarial suffix to bypass safety constraints. Operating in a strict black-box setting, our method requires no access to model parameters or internals, thereby reflecting realistic threat scenarios in deployed systems. Through the iterative application of selection, mutation, and crossover heuristics, the framework systematically explores the discrete prompt space to identify high-fitness adversarial suffixes. Empirical findings reveal critical shortcomings in existing safety enforcement mechanisms and confirm the effectiveness and practical viability of the proposed attack.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GAS-Leak-LLM：基于遗传算法的黑箱LLM越狱后缀优化
大型语言模型（LLMs）是AI主导的信息技术生态系统中的关键组成部分。为了减轻与有害或违反政策输出相关的风险，商业系统采用先进的对齐策略和多层次内容审核机制。尽管有这些保护措施，最近的研究表明，LLMs仍然容易受到对抗性操控，特别是通过越狱和提示注入技术。在本研究中，我们提出了GAS-Leak-LLM，一种基于遗传算法的新型越狱攻击，系统地演化对抗性后缀以绕过安全约束。在严格的黑箱环境中，我们的方法不需要访问模型参数或内部结构，从而反映了已部署系统中的现实威胁场景。通过选择、变异和交叉启发式的迭代应用，该框架系统地探索离散提示空间，以识别高适应性的对抗性后缀。实证研究揭示了现有安全执行机制的关键缺陷，并确认了所提攻击的有效性和实际可行性。

CHILLGuard: Towards Fine-Grained Chinese LLM Safety Guardrail with Scalable Data Construction and Model-aware Preference Alignment
Authors: Wenbo Yu, Bohua Wang, Hao Fang, Kuofeng Gao, Jingru Zeng, Xiaochen Yang, Tianyi Zhang, Xiaoxiao Ma, Jiawei Kong, Hao Wu, Bin Chen, Shu-Tao Xia, Min Zhang
First: 2026-06-13T16:57:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-13T16:57:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Malicious content generated from large language models (LLMs) could pose severe safety risks and ethical concerns. While existing LLM safety guardrails excel in English or multilingual settings, they lack adaptation to Chinese-specific regulatory policies, cultural context and linguistic nuances, failing to support fine-grained risk classification for diverse deployment needs. In this paper, we introduce a 5-macro, 31-micro category fine-grained risk taxonomy for Chinese scenarios, and build CHILLGuard: a dedicated Chinese LLM content safety guardrail. To address the critical scarcity of high-quality annotated Chinese safety data, we propose a scalable multi-stage data construction pipeline: we expand multi-source corpus via retrieval-augmented generation, generate implicit harmful samples through prompt engineering rewriting, and refine high-quality data via multi-model voting-based label calibration. Based on this, we build CHILLGuardTrain, a large-scale training set with 405,007 samples, and CHILLGuardTest, a rigorously curated annotated test set with 51,745 samples. We then train CHILLGuard on CHILLGuardTrain under a generator-classifier collaborative framework via Model-aware Direct Preference Optimization. Extensive experiments under multiple settings demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of CHILLGuard, e.g., a 15.92% improvement of F1 score over Qwen3Guard-8B-Strict on our benchmark. We will release our resources at https://github.com/cswbyu/CHILLGuard.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CHILLGuard：面向细粒度中文LLM安全防护的可扩展数据构建与模型感知偏好对齐
大型语言模型（LLMs）生成的恶意内容可能带来严重的安全风险和伦理问题。现有的LLM安全防护在英语或多语言环境中表现出色，但缺乏对中国特定监管政策、文化背景和语言细微差别的适应，无法支持多样化部署需求的细粒度风险分类。本文提出了一种针对中文场景的5个宏观、31个微观类别的细粒度风险分类法，并构建了CHILLGuard：一个专门的中文LLM内容安全防护。为了解决高质量标注中文安全数据的严重短缺，我们提出了一种可扩展的多阶段数据构建流程：通过检索增强生成扩展多源语料，通过提示工程重写生成隐性有害样本，并通过多模型投票的标签校准精炼高质量数据。在此基础上，我们构建了CHILLGuardTrain，一个包含405,007个样本的大规模训练集，以及CHILLGuardTest，一个经过严格策划的包含51,745个样本的标注测试集。然后，我们在CHILLGuardTrain上通过模型感知直接偏好优化的生成器-分类器协作框架训练CHILLGuard。多种设置下的广泛实验表明，CHILLGuard的性能达到了最先进水平，例如，在我们的基准测试中，F1分数比Qwen3Guard-8B-Strict提高了15.92%。我们将把我们的资源发布在https://github.com/cswbyu/CHILLGuard。

The methodology employs a generator-classifier collaborative framework with Model-aware Direct Preference Optimization, achieving state-of-the-art performance, including a 15.92% improvement in F1 score over the existing Qwen3Guard-8B-Strict benchmark, thereby demonstrating its capability to meet the specific safety needs of Chinese LLM applications.
本研究针对大型语言模型（LLMs）生成的恶意内容所带来的重大安全风险和伦理问题，特别是在中文语言和文化背景下，现有的安全防护措施显得不足。以往的方法主要集中在英语或多语言环境中，缺乏对中文特定监管政策和语言细微差别的适应，导致风险分类效果不佳。提出的方法CHILLGuard引入了针对中文场景的细粒度风险分类法，并采用可扩展的多阶段数据构建流程生成高质量的标注安全数据。该方法包括通过检索增强生成、提示工程生成有害样本以及多模型投票进行标签校准，最终形成了包含405,007个样本的大规模训练集和51,745个样本的测试集。实验结果表明，CHILLGuard在性能上达到最先进水平，在基准测试中F1分数比之前的基准提高了15.92%，有效填补了中文环境下LLM安全的空白。
Do You Really Need a GPU to Guard Your LLM? CPU-Class Classifiers and Multi-Stage Pipelines for Safety Enforcement at Scale
Authors: Vasudev Majhi, Dhruv Gupta, Advait Singh, Matthew Barker, Dhruv Kumar
First: 2025-12-22T04:00:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-13T05:46:54+00:00
Comments: Under Review. 25 pages, 5 figures, 38 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety classifiers that screen LLM inputs for jailbreak attempts have become standard deployment components, yet almost all production systems rely on GPU-based models: fine-tuned transformers and LLM-as-a-judge pipelines. These approaches impose significant per-query latency and infrastructure cost. Very little research has asked whether CPU-based classifiers, such as support vector machines and gradient-boosted trees trained on TF-IDF features, can match their accuracy across the conditions that production deployments encounter. We evaluate five CPU classifier families, Mamba-130M as an SSM-based GPU classifier, and transformer-based GPU models (DeBERTa-v3 and Gemma-2B with LoRA) across nine jailbreak sources and three regimes: in-distribution (D1), out-of-distribution (D2), and adversarially obfuscated (D3). On D1, the best CPU classifier matches the best transformer GPU model at roughly one-fifth the deployment cost. On D2, CPU classifiers fail via confident miscalibration, producing high-confidence false negatives that bypass escalation entirely. On D3, CPU classifiers outperform transformer GPU models by more than 26 percentage points in F1. Based on these complementary failure modes, we design GuardChain, a three-stage safety pipeline (Regex -> CPU -> GPU) that routes each prompt to the cheapest stage capable of a confident decision. The CPU stage alone resolves 80\% of in-distribution prompts at near-peak accuracy, and the GPU stage recovers the out-of-distribution failures. For practitioners deploying LLM safety at scale, this work provides evidence that GPU-class infrastructure is unnecessary for the majority of traffic.
中文标题/摘要
标题：您真的需要 GPU 来保护您的 LLM 吗？用于安全执行的 CPU 类分类器和多阶段管道
用于筛查 LLM 输入的安全分类器已成为标准部署组件，但几乎所有生产系统都依赖于基于 GPU 的模型：微调的变换器和 LLM 作为裁判的管道。这些方法在每个查询上都带来了显著的延迟和基础设施成本。很少有研究探讨基于 CPU 的分类器，如支持向量机和基于 TF-IDF 特征训练的梯度提升树，是否能在生产部署所遇到的条件下匹配其准确性。 我们评估了五个 CPU 分类器系列，Mamba-130M 作为基于 SSM 的 GPU 分类器，以及基于变换器的 GPU 模型（DeBERTa-v3 和 Gemma-2B 与 LoRA）在九个越狱来源和三个模式下的表现：分布内（D1）、分布外（D2）和对抗性混淆（D3）。在 D1 中，最佳 CPU 分类器的表现与最佳变换器 GPU 模型相当，部署成本约为其五分之一。在 D2 中，CPU 分类器因自信的错误校准而失败，产生高置信度的假阴性，完全绕过升级。在 D3 中，CPU 分类器在 F1 上超过变换器 GPU 模型超过 26 个百分点。 基于这些互补的失败模式，我们设计了 GuardChain，一个三阶段安全管道（Regex -> CPU -> GPU），将每个提示路由到能够做出自信决策的最便宜阶段。仅 CPU 阶段就以接近峰值的准确率解决了 80% 的分布内提示，而 GPU 阶段则恢复了分布外的失败。对于大规模部署 LLM 安全的从业者而言，这项工作提供了证据，表明 GPU 类基础设施对于大多数流量并非必要。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the growing need for effective safety classifiers that screen inputs for large language models (LLMs) against jailbreak attempts, which have traditionally relied on GPU-based models, leading to high latency and infrastructure costs. Previous methods predominantly utilized fine-tuned transformers, which are costly and inefficient for many deployment scenarios. The proposed approach introduces CPU-based classifiers, such as support vector machines and gradient-boosted trees, which are evaluated against GPU models across various conditions. The study finds that while CPU classifiers match GPU performance on in-distribution data at a significantly lower cost, they struggle with out-of-distribution data due to miscalibration. To mitigate these issues, the authors propose GuardChain, a multi-stage safety pipeline that effectively routes prompts to the most efficient classifier available, achieving 80% resolution of in-distribution prompts with high accuracy. NeST: Neuron Selective Tuning for LLM Safety
Authors: Sasha Behrouzi, Lichao Wu, Mohamadreza Rostami, Ahmad-Reza Sadeghi
First: 2026-02-18T20:01:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-12T11:06:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment is essential for the responsible deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs). Yet, existing approaches often rely on heavyweight fine-tuning that is costly to update, audit, and maintain across model families. Full fine-tuning incurs substantial computational and storage overhead, while parameter-efficient methods, e.g., Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), trade efficiency for inconsistent safety gains and sensitivity to design choices. Safety intervention mechanisms reduce unsafe outputs without modifying model weights, but do not directly shape or preserve the internal representations that govern safety behavior. We present NeST, a Neuron-Selective Tuning framework for efficient post-hoc safety alignment. NeST identifies safety-relevant feed-forward neurons via activation probing on vanilla harmful and benign prompts, clusters neurons with similar activation profiles, and trains shared cluster-level updates while freezing the rest of the model. Importantly, NeST is trained only on vanilla malicious prompts, without using jailbreak-specific attack data, yet generalizes robustly to diverse jailbreaks. The learned updates are then folded into the original weights, incurring no inference-time overhead. Evaluated on 14 open-weight language and multimodal models, NeST outperforms lightweight baselines and approaches full fine-tuning robustness with significantly fewer trainable parameters. On text-only models, NeST reduces average jailbreak attack success rate from 44.5% to 1.1% while training only 0.4M parameters on average. Across multimodal settings, it reduces ASR from 55.3% to 1.1%, and for downstream fine-tuned variants, it restores safety by reducing ASR from 53.8% to 0.8%. These results show that robust, maintainable safety alignment can be achieved by concentrating adaptation on localized, functionally coherent safety structures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：NeST：用于大型语言模型安全的神经元选择性调优
安全对齐对于大型语言模型（LLMs）的负责任部署至关重要。然而，现有方法通常依赖于成本高昂的重调优，难以在模型家族中进行更新、审计和维护。完全调优会产生大量的计算和存储开销，而参数高效的方法，如低秩适应（LoRA），则在效率与安全收益不一致和对设计选择敏感之间进行权衡。安全干预机制在不修改模型权重的情况下减少不安全输出，但并未直接塑造或保留影响安全行为的内部表示。 我们提出了NeST，一个用于高效事后安全对齐的神经元选择性调优框架。NeST通过对普通有害和良性提示的激活探测，识别与安全相关的前馈神经元，聚类具有相似激活特征的神经元，并在冻结模型其余部分的同时训练共享的聚类级更新。重要的是，NeST仅在普通恶意提示上进行训练，而不使用特定于越狱的攻击数据，但能够稳健地推广到多种越狱场景。学习到的更新随后被折叠到原始权重中，不会增加推理时的开销。在14个开放权重的语言和多模态模型上进行评估，NeST的表现优于轻量级基线，并以显著更少的可训练参数接近完全调优的鲁棒性。在仅文本模型上，NeST将平均越狱攻击成功率从44.5%降低到1.1%，同时平均仅训练0.4M参数。在多模态设置中，它将ASR从55.3%降低到1.1%，对于下游微调变体，它通过将ASR从53.8%降低到0.8%来恢复安全。这些结果表明，通过集中适应于局部、功能一致的安全结构，可以实现稳健、可维护的安全对齐。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for safety alignment in the deployment of Large Language Models (LLMs), highlighting the limitations of existing methods such as full fine-tuning and parameter-efficient approaches like Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA), which either incur high computational costs or fail to provide consistent safety improvements. The proposed NeST (Neuron-Selective Tuning) framework offers a novel solution by identifying safety-relevant neurons through activation probing and clustering them for targeted updates, allowing for efficient post-hoc safety alignment without modifying the entire model. This method is well-motivated as it aims to enhance safety while minimizing resource expenditure. The paper demonstrates that NeST significantly reduces the average success rate of jailbreak attacks on various models, achieving a drop from 44.5% to 1.1% on text-only models and from 55.3% to 1.1% in multimodal settings, while only training a small number of parameters, thus proving its effectiveness in maintaining robust safety alignment.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLM）部署中安全对齐的关键需求，强调现有方法的局限性，如全量微调资源消耗大，以及低秩适应（LoRA）等参数高效技术在安全一致性上的妥协。提出的NeST（神经元选择性调优）框架通过激活探测识别和调优仅与安全相关的神经元，提供了一种新颖的方法，实现高效的后期安全对齐，而无需修改整个模型。该方法的动机在于需要一种更可维护和有效的安全干预，能够在各种威胁中良好泛化。NeST在14个语言和多模态模型上进行了评估，表现出优越的性能，将平均越狱攻击成功率从44.5%降低到1.1%，同时平均仅训练0.4百万个参数，从而以最小的计算开销实现了稳健的安全对齐。
When Behavioral Safety Evaluation Fails: A Representation-Level Perspective
Authors: Enyi Jiang, Anders Gjølbye, Yibo Jacky Zhang, Sanmi Koyejo
First: 2026-06-06T08:10:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-06T08:10:56+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM) safety has often been evaluated at the behavior level, which provides limited evidence of internal robustness, as these evaluations target outputs rather than representation-level vulnerability under intervention. We formalize this discrepancy as the audit gap: the difference between behavioral safety and robustness under intervention. To study this gap, we construct dissociated models that preserve safe outward behavior while remaining vulnerable in the latent space. We introduce an intervention-based evaluation framework to test model robustness through soft interventions in parameter and latent spaces, including harmful fine-tuning and layer-wise latent perturbations. To formalize the evaluation, we propose the Latent Vulnerability Score (LVS) to measure how easily harmful behavior can be elicited by bounded latent perturbations. Using this evaluation framework, we show that behavioral safety metrics are insufficient measures of representation-level robustness across multiple safely and unsafely aligned state-of-the-art models. Notably, dissociated models show substantially elevated LVSs despite comparable refusal behavior under harmful intervention, with intermediate representations being the most sensitive to intervention. Our results suggest that behavioral safety evaluation alone provides an incomplete picture of model robustness, motivating representation-aware audits of latent vulnerability and observable behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：行为安全评估失败时：一种表征层面的视角
大型语言模型（LLM）的安全性通常在行为层面进行评估，这提供了有限的内部稳健性证据，因为这些评估针对的是输出，而不是干预下的表征层面脆弱性。我们将这种差异形式化为审计差距：行为安全与干预下的稳健性之间的差异。为了研究这一差距，我们构建了保持安全外部行为的分离模型，同时在潜在空间中保持脆弱性。我们引入了一种基于干预的评估框架，通过参数和潜在空间中的软干预来测试模型的稳健性，包括有害的微调和层级潜在扰动。为了形式化评估，我们提出了潜在脆弱性评分（LVS），以测量有害行为在有限潜在扰动下被引发的难易程度。使用该评估框架，我们表明行为安全指标不足以衡量多种安全和不安全对齐的最先进模型的表征层面稳健性。值得注意的是，尽管在有害干预下拒绝行为相当，分离模型的LVS显著升高，中间表征对干预最为敏感。我们的结果表明，仅依靠行为安全评估无法全面反映模型的稳健性，促使对潜在脆弱性和可观察行为进行表征意识审计。

Previous methods have primarily assessed behavioral safety, failing to capture the audit gap between observed behavior and latent robustness. This paper proposes a novel intervention-based evaluation framework that includes the introduction of the Latent Vulnerability Score (LVS) to quantify the susceptibility of models to harmful interventions in their latent space. The methodology involves constructing dissociated models and applying soft interventions to assess their robustness. The findings reveal that traditional behavioral safety metrics do not adequately reflect representation-level vulnerabilities, as evidenced by the significantly higher LVS in dissociated models, indicating a need for more comprehensive evaluation approaches that consider both latent and observable behaviors.

PreAct-Bench: Benchmarking Predictive Monitoring in LLMs
Authors: Hainiu Xu, Italo Luis da Silva, Jiangnan Ye, Yuhao Wang, Wei Liu, Linyi Yang, Jonathan Richard Schwarz, Nicola Paoletti, Yulan He, Hanqi Yan
First: 2026-06-03T13:26:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-03T13:26:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as autonomous agents capable of executing multi-step action trajectories toward a given objective. While existing safety research has focused on detecting unethical behavior from complete trajectories, this paradigm is fundamentally retrospective: it identifies harm only after it has already occurred. In this work, we study a critical yet overlooked safety task, which we term Predictive Monitoring: given only a partial action trajectory, can a model infer whether it will culminate in an unethical action before the overt action is executed? To support this task, we present PreActBench, a benchmark of 1,000 paired ethical and unethical action trajectories spanning five domains. We evaluate a range of LLMs, safety guardrail models, and latent probing methods across varying fractions of the action trajectory using our Prefix Foresight F1 metric. Results show that while humans achieve promising performance, predictive monitoring remains challenging even for strong models, highlighting the need for future-oriented risk reasoning in LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PreAct-Bench：大语言模型预测监控基准测试
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地被部署为能够执行多步骤行动轨迹以实现特定目标的自主代理。虽然现有的安全研究集中在检测完整轨迹中的不道德行为，但这种范式在根本上是回顾性的：它仅在伤害发生后才进行识别。在本研究中，我们研究了一个关键但被忽视的安全任务，我们称之为预测监控：仅给定部分行动轨迹，模型能否推断出它是否会在显性行动执行之前以不道德行为告终？为支持这一任务，我们提出了PreAct-Bench，这是一个涵盖五个领域的1,000对伦理和不伦理行动轨迹的基准测试。我们使用我们的Prefix Foresight F1指标评估了一系列LLMs、安全护栏模型和潜在探测方法在不同的行动轨迹分数下的表现。结果表明，尽管人类表现出良好的性能，但即使对于强模型，预测监控仍然具有挑战性，突显了LLM安全中未来导向风险推理的必要性。

The research addresses the growing deployment of large language models (LLMs) as autonomous agents and the limitations of existing safety measures that focus on retrospective detection of unethical behavior after it occurs. Previous methods have primarily identified harm post-action, which does not prevent unethical actions. This paper introduces a novel approach called Predictive Monitoring, which aims to determine the potential for unethical actions based on partial action trajectories before they are executed. The authors present PreAct-Bench, a benchmark consisting of 1,000 ethical and unethical action trajectory pairs across five domains, and evaluate various LLMs and safety models using the Prefix Foresight F1 metric. The findings reveal that while human performance is promising, predictive monitoring remains a significant challenge for even advanced models, underscoring the necessity for proactive risk assessment in LLM safety.

TamperBench: Systematically Stress-Testing LLM Safety Under Fine-Tuning and Tampering
Authors: Saad Hossain, Tom Tseng, Punya Syon Pandey, Samanvay Vajpayee, Matthew Kowal, Nayeema Nonta, Samuel Simko, Stephen Casper, Zhijing Jin, Kellin Pelrine, Sirisha Rambhatla
First: 2026-02-06T18:04:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T23:27:30+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 15 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
As increasingly capable open-weight large language models (LLMs) are deployed, improving their tamper resistance against unsafe modifications, whether accidental or intentional, becomes critical to minimize risks. However, there is no standard approach to evaluate tamper resistance. Varied datasets, metrics, and tampering configurations make it difficult to compare safety, utility, and robustness across different models and defenses. To address this, we introduce TamperBench, the first unified framework to systematically evaluate the tamper resistance of LLMs. TamperBench (i) curates a repository of state-of-the-art weight-space fine-tuning attacks, latent-space representation attacks, and alignment-stage defenses; (ii) enables realistic adversarial evaluation through systematic hyperparameter sweeps per attack-model pair; and (iii) provides both safety and utility evaluations. We use TamperBench to evaluate 21 open-weight LLMs, including defense-augmented variants, across nine tampering threats using standardized safety and capability metrics with hyperparameter sweeps per model-attack pair. The results provide insights including effects of post-training on tamper resistance, that jailbreak-tuning is typically the most severe attack, and that current alignment-stage defenses largely fail to withstand attack sweeps. Code is available at https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TamperBench：系统性压力测试LLM在微调和篡改下的安全性
随着越来越强大的开放权重大型语言模型（LLM）的部署，提高其对意外或故意不安全修改的抗篡改能力变得至关重要，以最小化风险。然而，目前没有标准的方法来评估抗篡改能力。不同的数据集、指标和篡改配置使得比较不同模型和防御的安全性、实用性和鲁棒性变得困难。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了TamperBench，这是第一个统一框架，用于系统性评估LLM的抗篡改能力。TamperBench (i) 汇集了最先进的权重空间微调攻击、潜在空间表示攻击和对齐阶段防御的库；(ii) 通过对每个攻击-模型对进行系统的超参数搜索，启用现实的对抗性评估；(iii) 提供安全性和实用性评估。我们使用TamperBench评估了21个开放权重LLM，包括增强防御的变体，针对九种篡改威胁使用标准化的安全性和能力指标，并对每个模型-攻击对进行超参数搜索。结果提供了包括后训练对抗篡改能力的影响、越狱微调通常是最严重的攻击，以及当前对齐阶段防御在抵御攻击搜索方面大多失败的见解。代码可在https://github.com/criticalml-uw/TamperBench获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical need for improved tamper resistance in large language models (LLMs) as their deployment increases, highlighting the lack of standardized methods for evaluating this resistance. Previous approaches have been hindered by inconsistent datasets, metrics, and tampering configurations, making comparisons across models challenging. The proposed TamperBench framework distinguishes itself by providing a unified system to evaluate LLM tamper resistance through curated attacks and systematic hyperparameter sweeps, thereby addressing the inconsistencies of past methods. This paper contributes by offering a comprehensive repository of fine-tuning attacks and defenses, enabling realistic adversarial evaluations. Using TamperBench, the authors evaluated 21 open-weight LLMs against nine tampering threats, revealing that jailbreak-tuning poses the most significant risk and that existing defenses are largely ineffective, thus supporting the need for improved safety measures in LLMs.
本研究解决了随着大型语言模型（LLMs）部署增加而对其抗篡改能力评估的迫切需求，强调了缺乏标准化评估方法的问题。以往的方法由于数据集、指标和配置的多样性而不一致，使得比较模型的安全性和鲁棒性变得困难。提出的TamperBench框架通过提供一个统一的系统，整理了微调攻击和防御，能够通过超参数搜索进行系统评估，从而克服了这些问题。本文的贡献在于系统评估了21个开放权重的LLM在九种篡改威胁下的表现，揭示了如越狱微调的严重影响以及当前防御措施的不足。该方法论表明，TamperBench能够有效评估安全性和实用性，支持增强LLM抗篡改能力的目标。
When Autoregressive Consistency Hurts Safety Alignment
Authors: Bochen Lyu, Yiyang Jia, Xiaohao Cai, Zhanxing Zhu
First: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T19:32:23+00:00
Comments: 21 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment in large language models (LLMs) is fragile in part because it is often shallow: fine-tuning mainly reshapes the model's behavior near the first few output tokens. We argue that this phenomenon can be understood through autoregressive consistency, the tendency of next-token prediction to preserve and extend the current response trajectory consistently. By analyzing the learning dynamics of safety alignment, we show that autoregressive consistency can concentrate alignment updates on early tokens, offering a mechanistic explanation for shallow safety alignment. The same mechanism also predicts a broader class of attacks on LLMs: attacks that induce harmful continuation states at arbitrary positions in the output trajectory. As a concrete example, we introduce random insertion attack, which inserts a short harmful span into an otherwise safe refusal trajectory and exploits autoregressive consistency to sustain the resulting harmful branch, thereby bypassing safety alignment. Notably, a short harmful span can redirect the generation to be harmful even after a long refusal prefix, highlighting autoregressive consistency as a potential broader failure mechanism. This suggests that safety alignment should also break harmful autoregressive consistency throughout the output trajectory. We therefore propose adversarial safety alignment, an initial framework based on worst-case harmful continuation states, and instantiate it with random worst-insertion training. Overall, our results suggest that autoregressive consistency should be treated as a central consideration in both safety alignment and attack design.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自回归一致性如何损害安全对齐
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐脆弱，部分原因在于其通常较浅：微调主要重塑模型在前几个输出标记附近的行为。我们认为，这一现象可以通过自回归一致性来理解，即下一个标记预测保持并延续当前响应轨迹的一致性倾向。通过分析安全对齐的学习动态，我们表明自回归一致性可以将对齐更新集中在早期标记上，为浅层安全对齐提供了机制性解释。同样的机制也预测了一类更广泛的对LLMs的攻击：在输出轨迹的任意位置诱导有害延续状态的攻击。作为具体例子，我们引入随机插入攻击，该攻击将一个短的有害片段插入到原本安全的拒绝轨迹中，并利用自回归一致性来维持由此产生的有害分支，从而绕过安全对齐。值得注意的是，一个短的有害片段可以在长拒绝前缀后重新引导生成变得有害，突显自回归一致性作为潜在的更广泛失败机制。这表明安全对齐也应打破输出轨迹中有害的自回归一致性。因此，我们提出了对抗性安全对齐，这是一个基于最坏情况有害延续状态的初步框架，并通过随机最坏插入训练进行实例化。总体而言，我们的结果表明，自回归一致性应被视为安全对齐和攻击设计中的核心考虑。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the fragility of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which is often limited to the initial output tokens due to autoregressive consistency. Previous methods primarily focused on fine-tuning, leading to shallow safety alignment that can be easily compromised. The proposed approach, adversarial safety alignment, aims to mitigate this issue by considering harmful continuation states throughout the output trajectory, rather than just at the beginning. This method introduces random worst-insertion training to enhance safety alignment against potential attacks, such as the random insertion attack, which can exploit autoregressive consistency to produce harmful outputs even after safe prefixes. The findings indicate that treating autoregressive consistency as a critical factor can improve both safety alignment and the design of defenses against attacks, thereby contributing to more robust LLM safety mechanisms.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）中安全对齐的脆弱性，这种脆弱性通常是由于微调主要影响初始输出标记而导致的。以往的方法集中于自回归一致性，导致对齐更新集中在早期标记上，未能确保输出的稳健安全。提出的方法对抗性安全对齐旨在通过考虑最坏情况的有害延续状态并采用随机最坏插入训练来缓解这些问题。这种方法揭示了短暂的有害插入可以在安全前缀之后将模型的输出重定向为不安全内容，从而强调了全面处理安全对齐的必要性。研究结果表明，解决自回归一致性问题对于增强LLMs的安全性和开发有效的攻击策略至关重要。
Black-box, Adaptive, Efficient, Transferable, Harmful, Applicable... Attacks Are All You Need to Break LLMs
Authors: Vincent Limbach, Jonas Dornbusch, David Lüdke, Stephan Günnemann, Leo Schwinn
First: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-06-02T13:39:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accurately evaluating adversarial robustness is a longstanding challenge. A flawed attack design can inflate robustness estimates, making deployment risk assessment and defense comparison unreliable. Historically, standardized attacks such as AutoAttack have largely resolved this for image classifiers, providing a reliable evaluation baseline for systematic comparison across defenses. However, no equivalent exists for LLM jailbreak evaluation yet, where designing such an attack is considerably more difficult. A reliable attack must, among other things, be black-box compatible, applicable to arbitrary defense pipelines, and efficient, which no existing method jointly satisfies. We introduce Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), a masked diffusion language model attacker trained via iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, requiring only black-box access to the target. The same method can be used without modification as a strong adaptive attack on individual behaviors, or as an efficient amortized policy that transfers to held-out behaviors and unseen target models without fine-tuning. Even against layered defenses, such as a Circuit Breaker-trained model combined with an auxiliary detector, IHO improves attack success considerably over state-of-the-art approaches, without any defense-specific adaptation. Our results position IHO as a practical step toward the kind of standardized jailbreak evaluation that has improved reliability in the past. Code and models are available on GitHub and Hugging Face.
中文标题/摘要
标题：黑箱、自适应、高效、可转移、有害、适用……攻击是破解LLM所需的一切
准确评估对抗鲁棒性一直是一个长期挑战。设计不当的攻击可能会夸大鲁棒性估计，使得部署风险评估和防御比较不可靠。历史上，标准化攻击如AutoAttack在图像分类器中基本解决了这一问题，为系统比较提供了可靠的评估基准。然而，目前尚无等效的LLM越狱评估标准，设计这样的攻击要困难得多。一个可靠的攻击必须在许多方面兼容黑箱，适用于任意防御管道，并且高效，而现有方法没有一个能够共同满足这些要求。我们引入了间接有害优化（IHO），这是一种通过迭代偏好优化训练的掩蔽扩散语言模型攻击者，仅需对目标进行黑箱访问。相同的方法可以在不修改的情况下作为对个体行为的强自适应攻击，或作为一种高效的摊销策略，能够转移到保留行为和未见目标模型上，而无需微调。即使面对分层防御，如与辅助检测器结合的电路断路器训练模型，IHO在攻击成功率上显著超越了最先进的方法，而无需任何特定于防御的适应。我们的结果将IHO定位为朝着标准化越狱评估的实用步骤，这在过去提高了可靠性。代码和模型可在GitHub和Hugging Face上获取。

Previous approaches have struggled to design effective attacks that are black-box compatible, applicable across various defense mechanisms, and efficient, leading to unreliable robustness estimates. The proposed method, Indirect Harm Optimization (IHO), overcomes these limitations by utilizing a masked diffusion language model attacker trained through iterative preference optimization against a harmfulness judge, requiring only black-box access to the target. IHO serves as both a strong adaptive attack on individual behaviors and an efficient policy that transfers to new behaviors and unseen models without fine-tuning. The experimental results demonstrate that IHO significantly enhances attack success rates against layered defenses compared to state-of-the-art methods, marking a significant advancement toward standardized jailbreak evaluation for LLMs.

D-Judge: Disrupting Multi-Turn Jailbreaks using Semantics-Preserving Output Rewriting
Authors: Huanli Gong, Zhipeng Wei, Yu Fu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Ananya Gupta, Yue Dong, N. Benjamin Erichson
First: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-31T06:40:02+00:00
Comments: Proceedings of the 43rd International Conference on Machine Learning
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn jailbreak attacks pose a growing threat to large language model (LLM) safety because they exploit feedback from auxiliary judge models to iteratively refine prompts toward harmful goals. Existing defenses largely detect or block unsafe content at individual turns or at the final response, leaving the judge-driven refinement loop intact and allowing attackers to extract informative feedback from intermediate interactions. We introduce D-Judge, a semantics-preserving output rewriting defense that intervenes directly in this loop by rewriting the victim LLM's responses before they are evaluated by the attacker's judge. By misaligning the judge's feedback signal without changing the meaning of the original response, D-Judge derails the attacker's prompt-refinement process, causing subsequent queries to be optimized against a distorted signal of attack progress. To improve D-Judge's ability to produce such rewrites, we construct a dataset of semantically equivalent response pairs that induce different judge-assigned harmfulness scores, and use it for supervised fine-tuning followed by direct preference optimization. Experiments on HarmBench show that D-Judge reduces the success rate of state-of-the-art multi-turn jailbreaks while preserving performance on benign benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：D-Judge：通过语义保持输出重写来破坏多轮越狱攻击
多轮越狱攻击对大型语言模型（LLM）的安全构成日益严重的威胁，因为它们利用辅助评判模型的反馈，迭代地优化提示以达到有害目标。现有防御主要在单个回合或最终响应中检测或阻止不安全内容，保持评判驱动的优化循环不变，使攻击者能够从中间交互中提取有用反馈。我们提出了D-Judge，这是一种语义保持输出重写防御，直接干预这一循环，通过在攻击者的评判之前重写受害者LLM的响应。通过在不改变原始响应含义的情况下使评判的反馈信号失真，D-Judge使攻击者的提示优化过程偏离轨道，导致后续查询针对扭曲的攻击进展信号进行优化。为了提高D-Judge生成此类重写的能力，我们构建了一个语义等价响应对的数据集，这些响应对引发不同的评判分配有害性评分，并利用该数据集进行监督微调，随后进行直接偏好优化。在HarmBench上的实验表明，D-Judge在保持良性基准性能的同时，降低了最先进的多轮越狱攻击的成功率。

This method is well-motivated as it directly targets the vulnerabilities in existing defenses. The contribution of the paper lies in the development of a dataset for supervised fine-tuning and preference optimization, which enhances D-Judge's ability to produce effective rewrites. Experimental results on HarmBench demonstrate that D-Judge significantly reduces the success rate of advanced multi-turn jailbreaks while maintaining performance on benign tasks.

Quality-Diversity Evolution for Discovering Diverse Vulnerabilities in LLM Safety
Authors: Subhadip Mitra
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-05-30T16:40:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T16:40:24+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 6 figures. Accepted at the ICLR 2026 Workshop on Agents in the Wild (AIWILD)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Current approaches to LLM adversarial testing suffer from coverage gaps: manual red-teaming does not scale, LLM-as-attacker methods exhibit mode collapse, and gradient-based approaches produce uninterpretable gibberish. We introduce a quality-diversity evolutionary framework that operates at the semantic level, evolving interpretable attack strategies rather than token sequences. Using MAP-Elites, we maintain a diverse archive of attacks across behavioral dimensions (strategy type, encoding method, prompt length). In experiments across GPT-4o-mini, Claude 3.5 Sonnet, Gemini 2.0 Flash, and an open-weight coding model (Devstral-small-2), we discover distinct vulnerability profiles: GPT-4o-mini is vulnerable to hypothetical and multi-turn framing combined with ROT13 encoding (fitness 0.8), Gemini to direct attacks with ROT13 and multi-turn with Leetspeak (0.8), while Claude shows uniformly ambiguous responses across all strategies (max 0.4). The semantic representation produces interpretable attacks that reveal systematic, model-specific weaknesses, providing actionable insights for improving LLM safety and a reproducible baseline for evaluating future frontier models. Code and experiment artifacts are released at https://github.com/bassrehab/red-queen.
中文标题/摘要
标题：质量-多样性进化用于发现LLM安全中的多样化脆弱性
当前LLM对抗测试的方法存在覆盖缺口：手动红队无法扩展，LLM作为攻击者的方法表现出模式崩溃，基于梯度的方法产生不可解释的乱码。我们引入了一种在语义层面操作的质量-多样性进化框架，进化可解释的攻击策略而非令牌序列。使用MAP-Elites，我们维护一个跨行为维度（策略类型、编码方法、提示长度）的多样化攻击档案。在对GPT-4o-mini、Claude 3.5 Sonnet、Gemini 2.0 Flash和一个开放权重编码模型（Devstral-small-2）的实验中，我们发现了不同的脆弱性特征：GPT-4o-mini对假设性和多轮框架结合ROT13编码（适应度0.8）脆弱，Gemini对直接攻击使用ROT13和多轮使用Leetspeak（0.8）脆弱，而Claude在所有策略中表现出均匀模糊的响应（最大0.4）。语义表示产生可解释的攻击，揭示系统性、模型特定的弱点，为改善LLM安全提供可操作的见解，并为评估未来前沿模型提供可重复的基线。代码和实验文物已发布在https://github.com/bassrehab/red-queen。

The Refusal--Compliance Tradeoff: A Large-Scale Safety Behavior Audit of Large Language Models
Authors: Alif Al Hasan, Sumon Biswas
First: 2026-05-06T20:35:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-30T15:07:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Refusal rates are a poor proxy for LLM safety, i.e., a model may over-refuse benign prompts while still complying with harmful ones. We audit both failure modes across 21 open-weight LLMs on four safety benchmarks (OR-Bench, XSTest, ToxiGen, BOLD), using a composition adjustment to isolate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity confounds. We report three findings. First, models adopt fundamentally different calibration strategies: conservative ecosystems such as Llama suppress unsafe outputs at the cost of elevated over-refusals, while permissive ecosystems such as DeepSeek and Qwen preserve helpfulness but tolerate higher harmful compliance. Second, demographic protection is unequal: models over-protect prominent racial and religious groups, frequently refusing even benign prompts about them, while providing substantially weaker protection against disability-targeted attacks. Third, refusal and compliance tendencies are stable within model families across generations and scales, suggesting that post-training objectives shape safety behavior more than architecture. Our results call for joint, demographically-aware, and multi-judge safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：拒绝与合规权衡：大规模语言模型的安全行为审计
拒绝率是大型语言模型安全性的一个糟糕代理，即模型可能在过度拒绝良性提示的同时仍然对有害提示做出反应。我们在四个安全基准（OR-Bench、XSTest、ToxiGen、BOLD）上审计了21个开放权重的大型语言模型的这两种失败模式，使用组合调整来隔离模型敏感性与数据集毒性混淆。我们报告了三项发现。首先，模型采用根本不同的校准策略：保守生态系统如Llama在提高过度拒绝的代价下抑制不安全输出，而宽松生态系统如DeepSeek和Qwen则保持有用性但容忍更高的有害合规。其次，人口保护不平等：模型过度保护显著的种族和宗教群体，频繁拒绝关于它们的良性提示，而对残疾目标攻击提供的保护则明显较弱。第三，拒绝和合规倾向在模型家族中跨代和规模保持稳定，表明后训练目标比架构更能塑造安全行为。我们的结果呼吁进行联合、关注人口统计和多评审的安全评估。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the inadequacy of refusal rates as indicators of safety in large language models (LLMs), highlighting that models may refuse benign prompts while complying with harmful ones. Previous methods primarily focused on refusal rates without considering the context of prompts, leading to misleading assessments of model safety. The proposed approach involves a large-scale audit of 21 open-weight LLMs across four safety benchmarks, utilizing a composition adjustment to differentiate model sensitivity from dataset toxicity. The paper contributes by revealing distinct calibration strategies among models, demonstrating unequal demographic protections, and indicating that safety behavior is influenced more by post-training objectives than by model architecture. The methodology effectively assesses safety behavior, showing that models exhibit stable refusal and compliance tendencies, which supports the need for a more nuanced safety evaluation framework that is demographically aware and incorporates multiple judges.
本研究探讨了拒绝率作为大型语言模型（LLMs）安全性指标的不足，强调模型可能拒绝良性提示而对有害内容表示顺从。以往的方法缺乏对模型行为的细致理解，常常将拒绝与安全混为一谈，而本研究通过对21个开放权重的LLMs在四个安全基准上进行审计，采用组合调整技术来区分模型敏感性与数据集毒性，纠正了这一点。本文的贡献在于揭示模型表现出不同的校准策略，保守模型如Llama优先考虑安全性，但导致过度拒绝，而宽容模型如DeepSeek则保持有用性，但允许有害的顺从。此外，研究发现保护水平在不同人群之间存在差异，并表明安全行为更多地受到后训练目标的影响，而非模型架构。所采用的方法论包括对模型对各种提示的响应进行全面审计，得出的见解倡导建立更为知情、关注人群的安全评估框架。
How Reliable Are AI Attackers Against a Fixed Vulnerable Target? A 400-Run Empirical Study of LLM Penetration Testing Consistency
Authors: Galip Tolga Erdem
First: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T15:39:43+00:00
Comments: 41 pages, 7 figures. Code and 400-run dataset: https://doi.org/10.5281/zenodo.20421592
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) can autonomously conduct multi-stage cyber attacks, but the consistency of their offensive behavior under repeated trials remains unstudied. This work presents the first large-scale empirical measurement of LLM attack consistency: 400 autonomous penetration testing runs (4 models, 100 each) against an identical honeypot hosting OWASP Juice Shop and two additional vulnerable services, holding prompt, orchestrator, and target constant. No model emitted a content refusal that survived the orchestrator's one-shot authorization re-prompt at iterations 0-1. Claude Sonnet 4's API calls did encounter upstream service unavailability - 91 of 1,135 calls returned HTTP 529 overloaded_error during a documented Anthropic capacity event, truncating 39 of 100 Claude runs. An earlier draft catalogued these as safety refusals; on full-log audit they are upstream API failures, not model-level refusals. Despite this, Claude achieved full exploitation in 61 of 100 runs; Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite in 85; GPT-4o-mini in 56 while deploying 98 unique attack strategies; qwen2.5-coder:14b in 25. Failure modes are model-distinctive: Claude through API truncation (39 runs), qwen through premature completion (52), GPT-4o-mini through iteration-budget exhaustion (23). Cross-service credential reuse appeared only in configurations retaining the most conversation history (qwen 57%, GPT-4o-mini 49%, cloud models 0% on 5-exchange windows). Cross-model exploitation rate differences are statistically significant (p < 0.001) with large effect sizes; qwen vs. Gemini SQL injection rates differ at Cohen's h = 1.12. First-exploit timing fell within a 15-30 second wall-clock range. To our knowledge, this is the first study to measure autonomous LLM attack behavior at N=100 per model across a multi-service target.
中文标题/摘要
标题：人工智能攻击者对固定脆弱目标的可靠性如何？一项关于大型语言模型渗透测试一致性的400次实证研究
大型语言模型（LLMs）可以自主进行多阶段网络攻击，但其在重复试验中的攻击行为一致性尚未研究。本研究首次大规模实证测量LLM攻击一致性：对一个托管OWASP Juice Shop和两个额外脆弱服务的相同蜜罐进行400次自主渗透测试（4个模型，各100次），保持提示、协调者和目标不变。在迭代0-1中，没有模型发出经过协调者一次性授权重新提示后仍然有效的内容拒绝。Claude Sonnet 4的API调用确实遇到了上游服务不可用的情况——在一次记录的Anthropic容量事件中，1,135次调用中有91次返回HTTP 529 overloaded_error，截断了100次Claude运行中的39次。早期草稿将这些列为安全拒绝；经过完整日志审计后，它们被认定为上游API故障，而非模型级拒绝。尽管如此，Claude在100次运行中实现了61次完全利用；Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite为85次；GPT-4o-mini为56次，同时部署了98种独特的攻击策略；qwen2.5-coder:14b为25次。失败模式具有模型特征：Claude通过API截断（39次运行），qwen通过过早完成（52次），GPT-4o-mini通过迭代预算耗尽（23次）。跨服务凭证重用仅出现在保留最多对话历史的配置中（qwen 57%，GPT-4o-mini 49%，云模型在5次交换窗口中为0%）。跨模型利用率差异具有统计显著性（p < 0.001），且效应量较大；qwen与Gemini的SQL注入率差异为Cohen's h = 1.12。首次利用的时间落在15-30秒的实际时间范围内。据我们所知，这是首个在多服务目标上对每个模型进行N=100的自主LLM攻击行为测量的研究。
Summary / 总结
This research investigates the consistency of large language models (LLMs) in conducting autonomous multi-stage cyber attacks, an area that has not been previously studied. Past methods lacked empirical measurement of attack consistency, leading to uncertainties regarding the reliability of LLMs in penetration testing. The proposed approach addresses these gaps by conducting a large-scale empirical study involving 400 autonomous penetration testing runs across four models against a fixed honeypot setup, maintaining constant conditions. The findings reveal significant differences in exploitation rates and failure modes among the models, with Claude achieving full exploitation in 61 out of 100 runs and qwen2.5-coder:14b in only 25. The study contributes to understanding LLM attack behavior by providing the first empirical measurement of their consistency across multiple services, demonstrating statistically significant differences in performance that support the research goals.
本研究探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在自主网络攻击中表现出的攻击行为的一致性，这是一个尚未被研究的话题。过去的方法缺乏对攻击一致性的实证测量，常常将API故障误分类为模型拒绝。所提出的方法涉及在固定的蜜罐环境中对四个LLM进行400次渗透测试，保持提示和协调器不变，从而允许对模型性能进行直接比较。研究发现模型之间的利用率和失败模式存在显著差异，其中Claude在61%的运行中实现了完全利用，而Gemini 2.5 Flash-Lite则为85%。这项工作通过提供关于LLM攻击一致性的首个大规模实证数据，为理解LLM在网络安全中的能力做出了贡献，支持了该领域进一步研究的必要性。
Beyond Attack Success Rate: Temporal Logit Observability for LLM Safety Failures
Authors: Junyoung Park, Sunghwan Park, Seongyong Ju, Jaewoo Lee
First: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T09:02:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Attack Success Rate (ASR) evaluates each jailbreak with a single yes/no label at the end of generation, telling us whether a failure happened but not how it unfolded. Two attacks that produce equally harmful outputs may have followed completely different paths, and ASR cannot tell them apart. We make those hidden paths observable from logits alone. Temporal Logit Observability (TLO) is a training-free diagnostic that watches a compliance-refusal margin during decoding and places each model-attack condition on a calibrated 2D plane. By design, this plane is most informative exactly where ASR is least informative: among attacks that succeed for genuinely different reasons. Across four aligned LLMs and three jailbreak paradigms, attacks with nearly identical ASR land at clearly different points on the plane: the same model can fail through different temporal patterns. The geometry matches refusal-direction probes from hidden states on most conditions, with one model showing the limit of our fixed-lexicon approach. A simple early-stop rule derived from TLO cuts successful jailbreaks by more than half, without false alarms on plain benign queries. Safety evaluation should report when and how a failure unfolds, not only whether it occurred. TLO makes the first two observable from logits alone.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越攻击成功率：LLM安全失败的时间逻辑可观察性
攻击成功率（ASR）在生成结束时用单一的是/否标签评估每个越狱，告诉我们是否发生了失败，但不说明其过程。两个产生同样有害输出的攻击可能遵循完全不同的路径，而ASR无法区分它们。我们使这些隐藏路径仅通过逻辑可观察。时间逻辑可观察性（TLO）是一种无训练的诊断方法，在解码过程中观察合规-拒绝边际，并将每个模型-攻击条件放置在一个校准的二维平面上。根据设计，这个平面在ASR信息最少的地方最具信息性：在因真正不同原因而成功的攻击之间。在四个对齐的LLM和三种越狱范式中，攻击几乎相同的ASR在平面上落在明显不同的点上：同一模型可以通过不同的时间模式失败。几何形状与大多数条件下隐藏状态的拒绝方向探测相匹配，其中一个模型显示了我们固定词汇表方法的极限。基于TLO得出的简单早停规则将成功的越狱减少了一半以上，而在普通良性查询上没有误报。安全评估应报告失败何时以及如何展开，而不仅仅是是否发生。TLO使前两者仅通过逻辑可观察。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of the Attack Success Rate (ASR) metric, which only indicates whether a jailbreak attack on large language models (LLMs) was successful without revealing the underlying processes. Previous methods have failed to differentiate between attacks that yield similar harmful outputs but follow different paths, leading to a lack of insight into model vulnerabilities. The proposed approach, Temporal Logit Observability (TLO), provides a training-free diagnostic that visualizes compliance-refusal margins during decoding, allowing for the observation of hidden paths in the attack process. This method is well-motivated as it enhances understanding of LLM safety failures by mapping model-attack conditions on a calibrated 2D plane, revealing distinct patterns even among attacks with identical ASR. The paper demonstrates that TLO can effectively reduce successful jailbreaks by over 50% with no false alarms on benign queries, thus contributing significantly to the safety evaluation of LLMs by emphasizing the importance of understanding the dynamics of failures rather than just their occurrence.
本研究解决了攻击成功率（ASR）指标的局限性，该指标仅指示模型失败是否发生，而未揭示导致失败的潜在过程。以往的方法，包括ASR，未能区分产生相似有害输出但路径不同的攻击，限制了其诊断效用。提出的方法，时间逻辑可观察性（TLO），提供了一种无训练的诊断工具，通过在校准的二维平面上可视化解码过程中的合规-拒绝边际，提供了对模型失败不同时间模式的洞察。本文的贡献在于证明TLO能够有效区分具有相同ASR但不同根本原因的攻击，在四个对齐的LLM和三种越狱范式中，成功减少了超过一半的成功越狱，同时在良性查询上未产生误报。这些发现表明，安全评估应关注失败的动态过程，而不仅仅是其发生，因为TLO允许对模型脆弱性进行更细致的理解。
Aligned but Fragile: Enhancing LLM Safety Robustness via Zeroth-Order Optimization
Authors: Zhihao Liu, Yifan Wu, Jian Lou, Di Wang, Yuxi Zhou, Yuke Hu
First: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:46:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment for large language models (LLMs) aims to reduce harmful or unsafe behavior while preserving general utility. However, recent findings reveal that alignment effects can be fragile: lightweight post-alignment manipulations, such as parameter noise, activation noise, or quantization, can easily weaken the intended safety behavior. Prior efforts to improve robustness have primarily focused on data curation, modified alignment objectives, and safety-critical parameter identification, leaving the role of the optimizer itself largely unexplored. In this paper, we are the first to study the robustness of safety alignment from the perspective of the base optimizer. This optimizer-centric view naturally points to zeroth-order optimization, which provides a robustness-oriented signal by evaluating safety alignment under perturbations. Based on this insight, we propose a hybrid framework that first performs standard first-order safety alignment and then applies zeroth-order refinement to improve robustness. Both theoretically and empirically, we show that only a few zeroth-order refinement steps can enhance robustness while preserving safety alignment. We further improve the efficiency of zeroth-order refinement by exploiting its inherent perturbation-based evaluations to estimate layer-wise robustness sensitivity, enabling the refinement process to concentrate updates on robustness-critical layers with modest training overhead.
中文标题/摘要
标题：对齐但脆弱：通过零阶优化增强大型语言模型的安全性鲁棒性
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全对齐旨在减少有害或不安全行为，同时保持一般效用。然而，最近的研究发现，对齐效果可能是脆弱的：轻量级的后对齐操作，如参数噪声、激活噪声或量化，可能会轻易削弱预期的安全行为。以往提高鲁棒性的努力主要集中在数据策划、修改对齐目标和安全关键参数识别上，而优化器本身的作用则大多未被探索。 在本文中，我们首次从基础优化器的角度研究安全对齐的鲁棒性。这种以优化器为中心的视角自然指向零阶优化，它通过在扰动下评估安全对齐提供了一个面向鲁棒性的信号。基于这一见解，我们提出了一个混合框架，首先执行标准的一阶安全对齐，然后应用零阶精炼以提高鲁棒性。我们理论和实证表明，仅需少量零阶精炼步骤即可在保持安全对齐的同时增强鲁棒性。我们进一步通过利用零阶精炼固有的基于扰动的评估来估计层级鲁棒性敏感性，提高了零阶精炼的效率，使精炼过程能够将更新集中在鲁棒性关键层上，且训练开销适中。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the issue of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which aims to mitigate harmful behaviors while maintaining overall utility. Previous methods have primarily concentrated on data curation and modified alignment objectives, but they often overlook the optimizer's role, leading to fragile safety behaviors that can be easily disrupted by minor perturbations. The proposed approach introduces an optimizer-centric perspective by utilizing zeroth-order optimization to enhance robustness, which is a novel contribution to the field. The methodology involves a hybrid framework that combines standard first-order safety alignment with zeroth-order refinement, demonstrating that minimal refinement steps can significantly improve robustness without compromising safety alignment. The experiments show that this method effectively enhances robustness while maintaining safety alignment, supporting the research goals of improving LLM safety.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）安全对齐的脆弱性，该对齐旨在减轻有害行为，同时保持实用性。以往的方法主要集中在数据整理和修改对齐目标上，忽视了优化器的作用，而本研究将其视为关键。所提出的方法引入了一种混合框架，结合了标准的一阶安全对齐和零阶优化，以增强对扰动的鲁棒性。该方法论表明，最少的零阶优化步骤可以显著提高鲁棒性，而不损害安全对齐，且实现了对关键层的高效更新，训练开销较低。研究结果表明，所提出的方法有效支持增强LLM安全鲁棒性的目标。
SelfGrader: LLM Jailbreak Detection via Anchored Token-Level Logits
Authors: Zikai Zhang, Rui Hu, Olivera Kotevska, Jiahao Xu
First: 2026-04-01T23:29:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-28T05:44:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are powerful tools for answering user queries, yet they remain highly vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing guardrail methods typically rely on internal features or textual responses to detect malicious queries, which either introduce substantial latency or suffer from randomness in text generation. To overcome these limitations, we propose SelfGrader, a lightweight guardrail method that formulates jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits. Specifically, SelfGrader evaluates the safety of a user query within a compact set of numerical tokens (NTs) (e.g., 0-9) and interprets their logit distribution as an internal safety signal. To align these signals with the target safety rubric, SelfGrader constructs Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and introduces a dual-perspective scoring rule that considers both the maliciousness and benignness of the query, yielding a stable and interpretable score that reflects harmfulness and reduces the false positive rate simultaneously. Extensive experiments across diverse jailbreak benchmarks, adaptive attacks, benign prompt benchmarks, multiple LLMs, and state-of-the-art guardrail baselines demonstrate that SelfGrader achieves strong robustness with low false positive rates, memory overhead, and latency.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SelfGrader：通过锚定的令牌级逻辑进行LLM越狱检测
大型语言模型（LLMs）是回答用户查询的强大工具，但它们仍然高度易受越狱攻击的影响。现有的防护方法通常依赖于内部特征或文本响应来检测恶意查询，这要么引入了显著的延迟，要么在文本生成中遭受随机性。为克服这些限制，我们提出了SelfGrader，这是一种轻量级的防护方法，将越狱检测公式化为使用锚定令牌级逻辑的数值评分问题。具体而言，SelfGrader在一组紧凑的数值令牌（NTs）（例如，0-9）中评估用户查询的安全性，并将其逻辑分布解释为内部安全信号。为了将这些信号与目标安全标准对齐，SelfGrader构建了可能近似正确引导的ICL锚定示例，并引入了一种双视角评分规则，考虑查询的恶意性和良性，从而产生一个稳定且可解释的分数，反映有害性并同时降低误报率。在多种越狱基准、适应性攻击、良性提示基准、多个LLM和最先进的防护基线上的广泛实验表明，SelfGrader在低误报率、内存开销和延迟方面实现了强大的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the vulnerability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks, highlighting the limitations of existing guardrail methods that rely on internal features or textual responses, which can introduce latency and randomness. The proposed approach, SelfGrader, differs by framing jailbreak detection as a numerical grading problem using anchored token-level logits, allowing for a more stable and interpretable evaluation of user queries. This method constructs Probably Approximately Correct-guided ICL anchor examples and employs a dual-perspective scoring rule to assess both malicious and benign queries, effectively reducing false positive rates. The methodology involves extensive experiments across various benchmarks and LLMs, demonstrating that SelfGrader achieves robust performance with low false positive rates, minimal memory overhead, and reduced latency, thereby supporting its goal of enhancing LLM safety.
