Jailbreaking and Mitigation of Vulnerabilities in Large Language Models
Authors: Benji Peng, Hanxuan Chen, Keyu Chen, Qian Niu, Ziqian Bi, Ming Liu, Pohsun Feng, Tianyang Wang, Lawrence K. Q. Yan, Yizhu Wen, Yichao Zhang, Caitlyn Heqi Yin, Xinyuan Song, Riyang Bao, Jiacheng Shi
Venue: Eureka 1(1) (2026) 26-61
First: 2024-10-20T00:00:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-27T16:38:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have transformed artificial intelligence by advancing natural language understanding and generation, enabling applications across fields beyond healthcare, software engineering, and conversational systems. Despite these advancements in the past few years, LLMs have shown considerable vulnerabilities, particularly to prompt injection and jailbreaking attacks. This review analyzes the state of research on these vulnerabilities and presents available defense strategies. We roughly categorize attack approaches into prompt-based, model-based, multimodal, and multilingual, covering techniques such as adversarial prompting, backdoor injections, and cross-modality exploits. We also review various defense mechanisms, including prompt filtering, transformation, alignment techniques, multi-agent defenses, and self-regulation, evaluating their strengths and shortcomings. We also discuss key metrics and benchmarks used to assess LLM safety and robustness, noting challenges like the quantification of attack success in interactive contexts and biases in existing datasets. Identifying current research gaps, we suggest future directions for resilient alignment strategies, advanced defenses against evolving attacks, automation of jailbreak detection, and consideration of ethical and societal impacts. This review emphasizes the need for continued research and cooperation within the AI community to enhance LLM security and ensure their safe deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型的越狱与漏洞缓解
大型语言模型（LLMs）通过推动自然语言理解和生成，改变了人工智能，使其在医疗、软件工程和对话系统等领域的应用得以实现。尽管近年来取得了这些进展，LLMs仍显示出相当大的脆弱性，特别是对提示注入和越狱攻击。本文回顾了这些漏洞的研究现状，并提出了可用的防御策略。我们大致将攻击方法分为基于提示、基于模型、多模态和多语言，涵盖对抗性提示、后门注入和跨模态利用等技术。我们还回顾了各种防御机制，包括提示过滤、转换、对齐技术、多智能体防御和自我调节，评估其优缺点。我们讨论了用于评估LLM安全性和鲁棒性的关键指标和基准，指出了在交互环境中量化攻击成功率和现有数据集偏见等挑战。识别当前研究空白，我们建议未来在弹性对齐策略、针对不断演变的攻击的高级防御、越狱检测的自动化以及伦理和社会影响的考虑等方面的研究方向。本文强调了在AI社区内持续研究和合作的必要性，以增强LLM安全性并确保其安全部署。

Got a Secret? LLM Agents Can't Keep It: Evaluating Privacy in Multi-Agent Systems
Authors: Aman Priyanshu, Supriti Vijay, Esha Pahwa
First: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T23:32:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM safety evaluations predominantly test models in isolation, yet deployed AI agents increasingly operate within persistent social environments alongside other agents. We introduce a Moltbook-style simulation platform where thousands of LLM agents interact across communities over a simulated month, and use it to evaluate privacy as a downstream safety concern under varying degrees of social pressure. We find that shifting from single turn to multi turn social evaluation amplifies privacy violations (CIMemories 19.95% to Ours 45.30% across OpenAI models), that leakage is socially contagious, with agents 8 times more likely to disclose sensitive information after observing a peer do so, and that explicit privacy instructions reduce but do not eliminate this effect, leaving leakage rates above 37.8% even with safeguards. Our findings suggest that static chat based safety benchmarks systematically underestimate risks in agentic deployment, and that social context alone is sufficient to elicit sensitive disclosures that single turn evaluations would never surface.
中文标题/摘要
标题：有秘密吗？LLM代理无法保密：多代理系统中的隐私评估
LLM安全评估主要在孤立环境中测试模型，但部署的AI代理越来越多地在与其他代理的持久社交环境中操作。我们引入了一种Moltbook风格的模拟平台，在该平台上，数千个LLM代理在模拟的一个月内跨社区互动，并利用它评估在不同社交压力下的隐私作为下游安全问题。我们发现，从单轮到多轮社交评估的转变会加剧隐私侵犯（CIMemories 19.95%到我们的45.30%，在OpenAI模型中），泄露是社交传染的，代理在观察到同伴泄露后泄露敏感信息的可能性增加8倍，并且明确的隐私指令虽然减少但并未消除这一效应，即使有保护措施，泄露率仍高于37.8%。我们的发现表明，静态基于聊天的安全基准系统性低估了代理部署中的风险，仅社交背景就足以引发敏感信息的披露，而单轮评估永远无法揭示这些信息。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the inadequacy of existing LLM safety evaluations, which typically assess models in isolation, failing to account for the complexities of multi-agent interactions in persistent social environments. Previous methods overlook the impact of social dynamics on privacy violations, leading to an underestimation of risks associated with deployed AI agents. The proposed approach utilizes a Moltbook-style simulation platform to observe thousands of LLM agents interacting over a simulated month, revealing that multi-turn evaluations significantly increase privacy violations and that social contagion plays a critical role in information leakage. The study's contributions highlight the limitations of static chat-based safety benchmarks and demonstrate that social context can trigger sensitive disclosures that single-turn evaluations miss. The methodology effectively evaluates privacy concerns under varying social pressures, achieving a leakage rate of 45.30% compared to 19.95% in traditional evaluations, indicating that existing safeguards are insufficient in real-world applications.
本研究解决了现有大型语言模型（LLM）安全评估的局限性，这些评估通常在孤立环境中进行，而不是在与其他代理共同操作的社会环境中。以往的方法未能考虑多代理交互的动态，导致隐私风险被低估。提出的Moltbook风格模拟平台允许在社区环境中对LLM代理进行评估，模拟一个月的时间，结果显示多轮社交评估显著增加了隐私违规行为。研究表明，代理在观察到同伴泄露敏感信息后，更有可能自己也进行泄露，尽管明确的隐私指令可以减少泄露，但并不能完全消除，泄露率仍超过37.8%。这些发现表明，传统的安全基准不足以理解代理部署中的风险，强调了在多代理系统中评估隐私问题时社会背景的重要性。
Evolving and Detecting Multi-Turn Deception using Geometric Signatures
Authors: Surender Suresh Kumar, Mary L. Cummings
First: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-26T20:48:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety defenses for large language models (LLMs) are typically trained and evaluated on single-turn prompts, yet real attacks often unfold as indirect, multi-turn probing. To defend against this more nuanced form of deception, we present a unified pipeline that generates realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets via multi-objective genetic prompt optimization with co-evolving mutation operators. We validate this dataset through a human study, which also revealed that early generations yielded the most convincing deception and practical constraints such as adherence filtering and ordering effects. Using this data, we were able to detect deceptive attempts to access prohibited information using simple, explainable geometric signals in embedding space coupled with a lightweight feed-forward classifier. Three geometric features (angular coverage, distance ratio, and linearity) augmented with pairwise similarity statistics led to a compact predictive model that achieved consistently high recall (0.89) across base, reworded, and truncated (three-turn) scenarios, with test-time F1 ranging from 0.74-0.86. The results support a central hypothesis that multi-turn deceptive intent leaves a stable geometric footprint that enables lightweight, transparent screening without expensive end-to-end training. We further discuss responsible uses, limitations, and paths toward larger, more diverse human-evaluated datasets. The primary contribution to artificial intelligence is the multi-objective evolutionary framework for prompt generation, and the engineering application is the deployment of a lightweight geometric detection system for LLM safety infrastructure.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用几何特征演变和检测多轮欺骗
大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全防御通常在单轮提示上进行训练和评估，但真实攻击往往以间接的多轮探测形式展开。为了防御这种更微妙的欺骗形式，我们提出了一个统一的流程，通过多目标遗传提示优化与共同演变的变异操作生成现实的多轮欺骗问题集。我们通过人类研究验证了该数据集，研究还揭示了早期生成的欺骗最具说服力，以及遵循过滤和排序效应等实际限制。利用这些数据，我们能够使用简单、可解释的几何信号在嵌入空间中检测试图访问禁止信息的欺骗尝试，并结合轻量级前馈分类器。三个几何特征（角度覆盖、距离比和线性）与成对相似性统计相结合，形成了一个紧凑的预测模型，在基础、改写和截断（三轮）场景中实现了一致的高召回率（0.89），测试时F1值范围为0.74-0.86。结果支持一个中心假设，即多轮欺骗意图留下稳定的几何足迹，使得无需昂贵的端到端训练即可实现轻量、透明的筛选。我们进一步讨论了负责任的使用、局限性以及朝向更大、更具多样性的人类评估数据集的路径。对人工智能的主要贡献是用于提示生成的多目标进化框架，工程应用是为LLM安全基础设施部署轻量级几何检测系统。

Previous methods have struggled to effectively capture the nuances of multi-turn deception, leading to a need for a more sophisticated approach. The proposed method introduces a unified pipeline that utilizes multi-objective genetic prompt optimization to generate realistic multi-turn deceptive question sets, validated through human studies that highlighted the effectiveness of early generations. The methodology employs geometric signals in embedding space, combined with a lightweight feed-forward classifier, to detect deceptive attempts, achieving high recall rates (0.89) and F1 scores ranging from 0.74 to 0.86 across various scenarios. $D^2$-Monitor: Dynamic Safety Monitoring for Diffusion LLMs via Hesitation-Aware Routing
Authors: Aoxi Liu, Yupeng Chen, James Oldfield, Guanzhe Hong, Junchi Yu, Baoyuan Wu, Philip Torr, Adel Bibi
First: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-25T14:22:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the emergence of diffusion large language models (D-LLMs) as an alternative to autoregressive large language models (AR-LLMs), safety monitoring for D-LLMs remains largely unexplored. Unlike AR-LLMs, D-LLMs generate text through a multi-step denoising process, exposing intermediate hidden representations that may contain safety-relevant information unavailable in standard single-step monitoring setups. Motivated by the suitability of lightweight probes for always-on monitoring, we analyze which trajectory-level signals best indicate when such probes are likely to struggle. We find that the most informative signal is safety hesitation: intermediate hidden states repeatedly falling within a small margin of the probe's decision boundary. The number of such hesitation steps in D-LLM's trajectory predicts probe failure effectively, providing a proxy of sample difficulty. Building on this analysis, we propose $D^2$-Monitor, a bi-level safety monitor for D-LLMs. $D^2$-Monitor adopts a lightweight probe as an always-on monitor to jointly estimate hesitation and perform base classification. When the hesitation level exceeds a threshold, a more expressive but computationally heavier probe is activated. This dynamic routing mechanism allocates monitoring resources efficiently at test time. Evaluated on 3 datasets (WildguardMix, ToxicChat, OpenAI-Moderation) across 4 D-LLMs, $D^2$-Monitor achieves state-of-the-art performance with a compact parameter footprint ($\leq$ 0.85M parameters), and exhibits the best trade-off between effectiveness and efficiency relative to 8 baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$D^2$-监控器：通过考虑犹豫的动态安全监控扩散大语言模型
尽管扩散大语言模型（D-LLMs）作为自回归大语言模型（AR-LLMs）的替代品已出现，但对D-LLMs的安全监控仍然 largely 未被探索。与AR-LLMs不同，D-LLMs通过多步骤去噪过程生成文本，暴露出可能包含安全相关信息的中间隐藏表示，而这些信息在标准单步监控设置中不可用。基于轻量级探针适合于始终在线监控的动机，我们分析了哪些轨迹级信号最能指示这些探针可能遇到困难。我们发现，最具信息量的信号是安全犹豫：中间隐藏状态反复落在探针决策边界的小范围内。D-LLM轨迹中此类犹豫步骤的数量有效预测探针失败，提供了样本难度的代理。基于此分析，我们提出了$D^2$-监控器，这是一个针对D-LLMs的双层安全监控器。$D^2$-监控器采用轻量级探针作为始终在线监控器，联合估计犹豫并执行基础分类。当犹豫水平超过阈值时，将激活一个更具表现力但计算负担更重的探针。该动态路由机制在测试时有效分配监控资源。在3个数据集（WildguardMix、ToxicChat、OpenAI-Moderation）上评估4个D-LLMs，$D^2$-监控器以紧凑的参数占用（≤ 0.85M参数）实现了最先进的性能，并在相对于8个基线之间展现了最佳的有效性与效率的权衡。

Previous methods primarily focused on single-step monitoring, which fails to utilize the intermediate hidden representations of D-LLMs that can provide safety-relevant information. The proposed approach, $D^2$-Monitor, introduces a bi-level safety monitoring system that leverages lightweight probes for continuous monitoring and activates a more complex probe when safety hesitation is detected, thus efficiently allocating resources. This method is well-motivated as it effectively predicts probe failure based on the number of hesitation steps in the D-LLM's trajectory. Reflect-Guard: Enhancing LLM Safeguards against Adversarial Prompts via Logical Self-Reflection
Authors: Lixing Lin, Juli You, Yue Li, Luyun Lin, Yiqing Wang, Zhen Zhang, Moxuan Zheng
First: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:58:21+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 2 figures, and 4 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM) safety classifiers such as Llama Guard are effective at detecting overtly harmful prompts but remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that disguise malicious intent through role-play scenarios, fictional framing, and indirect requests. We present Reflect-Guard, a method that augments LLM-based safety classifiers with chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning. Our approach distills analytical reasoning from GPT-4o-mini into structured reflection annotations, then trains Llama-Guard-3-8B via QLoRA to generate logical self-reflections before issuing safety verdicts. Using only 1000 training examples and updating just 0.5% of model parameters (~42M), Reflect-Guard achieves substantial improvements on two challenging benchmarks. On WildGuardTest, F1 score improves from 0.770 to 0.842 (+7.2 pp), with recall on adversarial prompts increasing from 0.513 to 0.921 (+40.8 pp). On JailbreakBench, the attack success rate drops from 10.3% to 1.8%, representing an 82.5% relative reduction. These gains are especially pronounced on adversarial inputs, where the explicit reasoning step enables the model to see through obfuscation techniques that defeat standard pattern-matching approaches. Our results demonstrate that teaching safety classifiers to reason about adversarial intent, rather than simply classify surface patterns, is a promising direction for robust LLM safety.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Reflect-Guard：通过逻辑自我反思增强LLM对抗性提示的安全防护
大型语言模型（LLM）安全分类器如Llama Guard在检测明显有害提示方面有效，但仍然容易受到通过角色扮演场景、虚构框架和间接请求伪装恶意意图的对抗性越狱攻击的影响。我们提出了Reflect-Guard，这是一种通过参数高效微调增强LLM基础安全分类器的链式思维自我反思能力的方法。我们的方法将GPT-4o-mini的分析推理提炼为结构化反思注释，然后通过QLoRA训练Llama-Guard-3-8B，以在发出安全裁决之前生成逻辑自我反思。仅使用1000个训练示例并更新0.5%的模型参数（约4200万），Reflect-Guard在两个具有挑战性的基准测试中取得了显著改善。在WildGuardTest上，F1分数从0.770提高到0.842（+7.2个百分点），对抗性提示的召回率从0.513提高到0.921（+40.8个百分点）。在JailbreakBench上，攻击成功率从10.3%降至1.8%，相对减少82.5%。这些提升在对抗性输入上尤为明显，明确的推理步骤使模型能够看穿击败标准模式匹配方法的混淆技术。我们的结果表明，教导安全分类器推理对抗性意图，而不仅仅是分类表面模式，是增强LLM安全性的一个有前景的方向。

The proposed Reflect-Guard enhances LLM safety by integrating chain-of-thought self-reflection capabilities through parameter-efficient fine-tuning, allowing the model to reason about adversarial intent. Specifically, the F1 score on WildGuardTest increased from 0.770 to 0.842, and the attack success rate on JailbreakBench decreased from 10.3% to 1.8%, demonstrating the effectiveness of reasoning in enhancing LLM safety against adversarial prompts.

RouteScan: A Non-Intrusive Approach to Auditing MoE LLMs Safety via Expert Routing Telemetry
Authors: Bo Lv, Zhiheng Xu, KeDong Xiu, Ruyi Ding, Tianhang Zheng, Zhibo Wang, Kui Ren
First: 2026-05-24T02:06:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-24T02:06:44+00:00
Comments: 20 pages. Under submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures have become an increasingly important paradigm for scaling Large Language Models (LLMs). As MoE models are increasingly deployed in real-world services, safety auditing becomes necessary to verify whether these models produce or facilitate harmful behaviors during operation. However, existing content-based auditing methods typically require access to user prompts, model inputs, or generated outputs, potentially exposing sensitive user information and creating a fundamental tension between LLM safety and user privacy. On the other hand, we observe that, in MoE models, sparse expert routing maps different inputs to activate different expert-execution patterns, producing measurable footprints in low-level GPU execution telemetry. Inspired by this observation, we propose RouteScan, a non-intrusive auditing framework for detecting harmful behaviors through GPU-level expert routing telemetry. Specifically, RouteScan utilizes the number of active GPU threads allocated to expert modules during the prefilling phase as a discriminative micro-architectural fingerprint, and builds a lightweight detection pipeline that isolates cross-domain invariant risk indicators for the precise identification of malicious prompts. Comprehensive evaluations on open-source MoE LLMs with distinct routing designs demonstrate that RouteScan achieves strong generalization, with an AUROC exceeding 0.93 on unseen harmful domains and 0.96 under novel jailbreak wrappers. Moreover, empirical inversion tests show that the collected expert routing telemetry provides limited information for prompt reconstruction, suggesting a practical privacy advantage over content-based auditing methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RouteScan：通过专家路由遥测对MoE LLM安全性进行非侵入式审计的方法
混合专家（MoE）架构已成为扩展大型语言模型（LLM）的一个日益重要的范式。随着MoE模型在现实服务中的日益部署，安全审计变得必要，以验证这些模型在操作过程中是否产生或促进有害行为。然而，现有的基于内容的审计方法通常需要访问用户提示、模型输入或生成的输出，可能会暴露敏感用户信息，并在LLM安全性与用户隐私之间产生根本性紧张关系。另一方面，我们观察到，在MoE模型中，稀疏专家路由将不同输入映射到激活不同的专家执行模式，产生可测量的低级GPU执行遥测足迹。受此观察启发，我们提出了RouteScan，一个通过GPU级专家路由遥测检测有害行为的非侵入式审计框架。具体而言，RouteScan利用在预填充阶段分配给专家模块的活跃GPU线程数量作为区分性微架构指纹，并构建一个轻量级检测管道，隔离跨域不变风险指标，以精确识别恶意提示。对具有不同路由设计的开源MoE LLM的全面评估表明，RouteScan实现了强大的泛化能力，在未见有害领域的AUROC超过0.93，在新型越狱包装下达到0.96。此外，经验反演测试表明，收集的专家路由遥测提供的提示重建信息有限，表明相较于基于内容的审计方法具有实际的隐私优势。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing need for safety auditing in Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures used in Large Language Models (LLMs), which have become prevalent in real-world applications. Traditional content-based auditing methods pose privacy risks by requiring access to sensitive user data, creating a conflict between ensuring model safety and protecting user privacy. The proposed method, RouteScan, differs by utilizing GPU-level expert routing telemetry, which captures execution patterns without exposing user prompts or outputs. This approach is well-motivated as it allows for effective auditing while maintaining user confidentiality. The paper contributes a non-intrusive framework that leverages active GPU thread counts during the model's prefilling phase to identify harmful behaviors. Evaluations on various open-source MoE LLMs show that RouteScan achieves an AUROC of over 0.93 on unseen harmful domains and 0.96 under novel jailbreak wrappers, indicating its effectiveness in detecting risks while supporting privacy goals.

BarrierSteer: LLM Safety via Learning Barrier Steering
Authors: Thanh Q. Tran, Arun Verma, Kiwan Wong, Bryan Kian Hsiang Low, Daniela Rus, Wei Xiao
First: 2026-02-23T18:19:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-21T18:01:19+00:00
Comments: This paper introduces SafeBarrier, a framework that enforces safety in large language models by steering their latent representations with control barrier functions during inference, reducing adversarial and unsafe outputs
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Despite the strong performance of large language models (LLMs) across diverse tasks, their susceptibility to adversarial attacks and unsafe content generation remains a significant obstacle to deployment, particularly in high-stakes settings. Addressing this challenge requires safety mechanisms that are both practically effective and theoretically grounded. In this paper, we introduce BarrierSteer, a novel inference-time framework that improves response safety by embedding learned nonlinear safety constraints directly into the model's latent representation space. BarrierSteer treats hidden-state safety classifiers as Control Barrier Functions (CBFs), enabling constraint-guided steering of unsafe latent trajectories during generation. By composing multiple safety constraints through efficient constraint merging without modifying the underlying LLM parameters, BarrierSteer preserves model utility. We provide theoretical results showing that applying CBFs in the latent space yields a principled, modular, and computationally efficient approach for steering with respect to learned safety constraints, with guarantees conditional on the learned barriers capturing the intended safety property. Our extensive experimental results across multiple model families and datasets demonstrate that BarrierSteer substantially reduces adversarial attack success rates and unsafe generations, outperforming the existing method. The code is available in our \href{https://github.com/thanhquangtran/BarrierSteer}{GitHub repository}.

标题：BarrierSteer：通过学习障碍引导实现LLM安全
尽管大型语言模型（LLMs）在各种任务中表现出色，但它们对对抗性攻击和不安全内容生成的易感性仍然是部署中的重大障碍，特别是在高风险环境中。解决这一挑战需要既有效又有理论基础的安全机制。本文介绍了BarrierSteer，这是一种新颖的推理时框架，通过将学习到的非线性安全约束直接嵌入模型的潜在表示空间来提高响应安全性。BarrierSteer将隐藏状态安全分类器视为控制障碍函数（CBFs），使得在生成过程中能够对不安全的潜在轨迹进行约束引导。通过高效的约束合并组合多个安全约束，而不修改底层LLM参数，BarrierSteer保持了模型的实用性。我们提供了理论结果，表明在潜在空间中应用CBFs提供了一种原则性、模块化和计算高效的引导方法，能够根据学习到的障碍捕捉预期的安全属性。我们在多个模型系列和数据集上的广泛实验结果表明，BarrierSteer显著降低了对抗性攻击成功率和不安全生成，优于现有方法。代码可在我们的\href{https://github.com/thanhquangtran/BarrierSteer}{GitHub仓库}中获取。

Previous methods lacked effective safety mechanisms that are both practically applicable and theoretically sound, leading to vulnerabilities in LLM deployment. Revisiting Robustness for LLM Safety Alignment via Selective Geometry Control
Authors: Yonghui Yang, Wenjian Tao, Jilong Liu, Xingyu Zhu, Junfeng Fang, Weibiao Huang, Le Wu, Richang Hong, Tat-Sent Chua
First: 2026-02-07T03:46:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-21T07:39:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Safety alignment of large language models remains brittle under domain shift and noisy preference supervision. Most existing robust alignment methods focus on uncertainty in alignment data, while overlooking optimization-induced fragility in preference-based objectives. In this work, we revisit robustness for LLM safety alignment from an optimization geometry perspective, and argue that robustness failures cannot be addressed by data-centric methods alone. We propose \textit{ShaPO}, a geometry-aware preference optimization framework that enforces worst-case alignment objectives via selective geometry control over alignment-critical parameter subspace. By avoiding uniform geometry constraints, ShaPO mitigates the over-regularization that can harm robustness under distribution shift. We instantiate ShaPO at two levels: token-level ShaPO stabilizes likelihood-based surrogate optimization, while reward-level ShaPO enforces reward-consistent optimization under noisy supervision. Across diverse safety benchmarks and noisy preference settings, ShaPO consistently improves safety robustness over popular preference optimization methods. Moreover, ShaPO composes cleanly with data-robust objectives, yielding additional gains and empirically supporting the proposed optimization-geometry perspective. The code is available at https://github.com/liujilong0116/ShaPO.

大型语言模型的安全对齐在领域转移和噪声偏好监督下仍然脆弱。现有的大多数鲁棒对齐方法关注对齐数据的不确定性，而忽视了基于偏好的目标中由优化引起的脆弱性。在本研究中，我们从优化几何的角度重新审视LLM安全对齐的鲁棒性，并认为鲁棒性失败不能仅通过以数据为中心的方法来解决。我们提出了\textit{ShaPO}，一个几何感知的偏好优化框架，通过对对齐关键参数子空间的选择性几何控制来强制执行最坏情况对齐目标。通过避免均匀几何约束，ShaPO减轻了在分布转移下可能损害鲁棒性的过度正则化。我们在两个层面上实例化ShaPO：令牌级ShaPO稳定基于似然的替代优化，而奖励级ShaPO在噪声监督下强制执行奖励一致的优化。在多样的安全基准和噪声偏好设置中，ShaPO始终优于流行的偏好优化方法，提高了安全鲁棒性。此外，ShaPO与数据鲁棒目标良好组合，带来额外收益，并在经验上支持所提出的优化几何视角。代码可在https://github.com/liujilong0116/ShaPO获取。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenges of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which often fail under domain shifts and noisy preference supervision. Previous methods primarily focused on data-centric approaches that do not adequately address the optimization-induced fragility of preference-based objectives. The proposed method, ShaPO, introduces a geometry-aware preference optimization framework that selectively controls the geometry of alignment-critical parameter subspaces, thereby avoiding the pitfalls of over-regularization. This approach is well-motivated as it enhances robustness in alignment objectives. The methodology includes token-level and reward-level implementations of ShaPO, which have been tested across various safety benchmarks and noisy preference scenarios, demonstrating consistent improvements in safety robustness compared to existing preference optimization methods and supporting the proposed optimization-geometry perspective.

On-Policy Consistency Training Improves LLM Safety with Minimal Capability Degradation
Authors: Andy Han, Kristina Fujimoto, Avidan Shah, Kiet Nguyen, Kai Xu, Chen Yueh-Han, Ilia Sucholutsky, Rico Angell
First: 2026-05-20T23:56:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-20T23:56:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Aligned models can misbehave in several ways: they are often sycophantic, fall victim to jailbreaks, or fail to include appropriate safety warnings. Consistency training is a promising new alignment paradigm to mitigate such failures by training invariants into the model using contrastive input pairs. Existing consistency training procedures generate the supervision signal once, offline, and use supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to update the model. Unfortunately, the resulting models tend to merely memorize the surface forms of the training distribution and thus generalize poorly and regress in their capabilities. We introduce On-Policy Consistency Training (OPCT), a new consistency training approach where the objective is computed over the model's own responses to prompts, supervised by itself conditioned on corresponding contrastive prompts. We evaluate OPCT on three safety axes: sycophancy, jailbreaking, and safety awareness. Across three model families, OPCT outperforms its SFT counterpart on all safety desiderata. It nearly halves the sycophancy rate relative to baseline (8.1% vs. 15.4%, compared to 11.2% for SFT). Under an adaptive per-target attacker, OPCT holds jailbreak defense success near 99% on held-out jailbreak behaviors, whereas SFT achieves 87% on average. On safety awareness, OPCT outperforms SFT in two out of three models, and matches it on the other. OPCT also largely avoids the capability regressions that SFT induces, such as a 28-point drop on MATH-500. Our results suggest that consistency training is best implemented as OPCT rather than as SFT, especially when generalization beyond the training distribution is desired.
中文标题/摘要

对齐模型可能以多种方式表现不当：它们往往表现得过于谄媚，容易受到越狱攻击，或未能包含适当的安全警告。一致性训练是一种有前景的新对齐范式，通过使用对比输入对将不变性训练到模型中，以减轻这些失败。现有的一致性训练程序仅在离线状态下生成一次监督信号，并使用监督微调（SFT）来更新模型。不幸的是，结果模型往往仅仅记住训练分布的表面形式，因此泛化能力差，能力退化。我们引入了基于策略的一致性训练（OPCT），这是一种新的一致性训练方法，其目标是基于模型对提示的自身响应进行计算，由相应的对比提示进行自我监督。我们在三个安全维度上评估OPCT：谄媚、越狱和安全意识。在三种模型系列中，OPCT在所有安全要求上均优于其SFT对应物。与基线相比，谄媚率几乎减半（8.1%对15.4%，而SFT为11.2%）。在自适应每个目标攻击者下，OPCT在保留的越狱行为上保持近99%的越狱防御成功率，而SFT平均为87%。在安全意识方面，OPCT在三种模型中的两种上优于SFT，另一种则持平。OPCT还在很大程度上避免了SFT引起的能力退化，例如在MATH-500上下降28分。我们的结果表明，一致性训练最好以OPCT的形式实施，而不是SFT，特别是在希望超越训练分布进行泛化时。

CR4T: Rewrite-Based Guardrails for Adolescent LLM Safety
Authors: Heajun An, Qi Zhang, Vedanth Achanta, Jin-Hee Cho
First: 2026-05-20T18:16:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-20T18:16:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly embedded in adolescent digital environments, mediating information seeking, advice, and emotionally sensitive interactions. Yet existing safety mechanisms remain largely grounded in adult-centric norms and operationalize safety through refusal-oriented suppression. While such approaches may reduce immediate policy violations, they can also create conversational dead-ends, limit constructive guidance, and fail to address the developmental vulnerabilities inherent in adolescent-AI interactions. We argue that adolescent LLM safety should be framed not solely as a filtering problem, but as a socio-technical, developmentally aligned transformation problem. To operationalize this perspective, we propose Critique-and-Revise-for-Teenagers (CR4T), a model-agnostic safeguarding framework that selectively reconstructs unsafe or refusal-style outputs into ageappropriate, guidance-oriented responses while preserving benign intent. CR4T combines lightweight risk detection with domain-conditioned rewriting to remove risk-amplifying content, reduce unnecessary conversational shutdown, and introduce developmentally appropriate guidance. Experimental results show that targeted rewriting substantially reduces unsafe and refusal-oriented outcomes while avoiding unnecessary intervention on acceptable interactions. These findings suggest that selective response reconstruction offers a more human-centered alternative to refusal-centric guardrails for adolescent-facing LLM systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CR4T：基于重写的青少年大型语言模型安全防护
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地嵌入青少年的数字环境中，调解信息搜索、建议和情感敏感的互动。然而，现有的安全机制仍然主要基于成人中心的规范，并通过拒绝导向的压制来实现安全。虽然这种方法可能减少即时的政策违规，但也可能造成对话的死胡同，限制建设性指导，并未能解决青少年与人工智能互动中固有的发展脆弱性。我们认为，青少年LLM安全不应仅仅被视为过滤问题，而应被视为一个社会技术、发展对齐的转型问题。为了实现这一视角，我们提出了针对青少年的批评与修订（CR4T），这是一个模型无关的安全框架，选择性地将不安全或拒绝风格的输出重构为适龄的、指导导向的响应，同时保持良好的意图。CR4T结合轻量级风险检测与领域条件重写，以去除风险放大内容，减少不必要的对话中断，并引入发展适宜的指导。实验结果表明，针对性重写显著减少了不安全和拒绝导向的结果，同时避免了对可接受互动的不必要干预。这些发现表明，选择性响应重构为面向青少年的LLM系统提供了一种更以人为本的替代方案，取代了以拒绝为中心的防护措施。

Adaptive Probe-based Steering for Robust LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Junxi Chen, Junhao Dong, Xiaohua Xie
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-05-19T06:11:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-19T06:11:04+00:00
Comments: 19 pages, 13 figures, accepted by ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Recent work has demonstrated the potential of contrastive steering for jailbreaking Large Language Models (LLMs). However, existing methods rely on limited and inherently biased contrastive prompts and require laborious manual tuning of steering strength, limiting their robustness and effectiveness. In this paper, we leverage the idea of model extraction to guide the learned steering vectors to approximate the ideal one and propose tuning the steering strength adaptively based on contrastive activations' statistics. Experiments demonstrate that our method notably improves the effectiveness and robustness of probe-based steering, without any extra contrastive prompts or laborious manual tuning. Being an attack paper, this paper focuses on revealing the breakdown of fortified LLMs, raising the average harmfulness score from 6\% to 70\%. Our code is available at https://github.com/fhdnskfbeuv/adaptiveSteering.

LLM-Safety Evaluations Lack Robustness
Authors: Tim Beyer, Sophie Xhonneux, Simon Geisler, Gauthier Gidel, Leo Schwinn, Stephan Günnemann
First: 2025-03-04T12:55:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T17:54:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we argue that current safety alignment research efforts for large language models are hindered by many intertwined sources of noise, such as small datasets, methodological inconsistencies, and unreliable evaluation setups. This can, at times, make it impossible to evaluate and compare attacks and defenses fairly, thereby slowing progress. We systematically analyze the LLM safety evaluation pipeline, covering dataset curation, optimization strategies for automated red-teaming, response generation, and response evaluation using LLM judges. At each stage, we identify key issues and highlight their practical impact. We also propose a set of guidelines for reducing noise and bias in evaluations of future attack and defense papers. Lastly, we offer an opposing perspective, highlighting practical reasons for existing limitations. We believe that addressing the outlined problems in future research will improve the field's ability to generate easily comparable results and make measurable progress.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型安全评估缺乏稳健性

Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenges faced in safety alignment research for large language models (LLMs), which are often affected by noise from small datasets, methodological inconsistencies, and unreliable evaluation setups. Previous methods have struggled with these issues, leading to difficulties in fairly evaluating and comparing attacks and defenses. This contribution aims to enhance the comparability of results and facilitate measurable progress in the field. The methodology involves a comprehensive examination of dataset curation, optimization strategies, response generation, and evaluation using LLM judges, ultimately aiming to improve the robustness of safety evaluations in LLM research.
本文的研究背景强调了大型语言模型（LLM）安全对齐研究面临的挑战，特别是由于小数据集、方法不一致和不可靠的评估设置带来的噪声。以往的方法在这些问题上存在困难，导致公平评估和比较攻击与防御的难度，从而阻碍了该领域的进展。提出的方法系统分析了LLM安全评估流程，识别出每个阶段的关键问题，并提供减少未来评估中噪声和偏差的指导方针。本文的贡献在于其全面的分析和提供的实用建议，旨在增强安全评估的稳健性。该方法论涉及对数据集策划、优化策略、响应生成和使用LLM评估的全面审查，最终旨在改善结果的可比性，并促进LLM安全研究的可测量进展。
Babel: Jailbreaking Safety Attention via Obfuscation Distribution Optimized Sampling
Authors: Ziwei Wang, Jing Chen, Ruichao Liang, Zhi Wang, Yebo Feng, Ju Jia, Ruiying Du, Cong Wu, Yang Liu
First: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite rigorous safety alignment, Large Language Models (LLMs) remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing black-box methods often rely on heuristic templates or exhaustive trials, lacking mechanistic interpretability and query efficiency. In this study, we investigate an intrinsic vulnerability in the safety mechanisms of LLMs, where safety alignment relies on a small set of sparsely distributed attention heads, leaving much of the representational space weakly monitored. We formalize this phenomenon with a mathematical jailbreaking model that characterizes the delicate boundary of effective text obfuscation and analytically explains observed jailbreak behaviors. Guided by this model, we propose Babel, an efficient black-box attack framework that exploits the identified safety gap through systematic obfuscation sampling with iterative, feedback-driven distribution refinement, enabling reliable and high-success jailbreak attacks without access to model internals. Comprehensive evaluations on frontier commercial models demonstrate that Babel achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates and superior query efficiency. Specifically, compared to state-of-the-art methods, Babel increases the attack success rate on GPT-4o from 41.33% to 82.67% and on Claude-3-5-haiku from 38.33% to 78.33% within an average of 40 queries, providing a robust red-teaming methodology for LLMs safety research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巴别尔：通过模糊分布优化采样破解安全注意力
尽管进行了严格的安全对齐，大型语言模型（LLMs）仍然容易受到越狱攻击。现有的黑箱方法通常依赖于启发式模板或穷举试验，缺乏机制可解释性和查询效率。在本研究中，我们调查了LLMs安全机制中的内在脆弱性，其中安全对齐依赖于一小组稀疏分布的注意力头，导致大部分表征空间监控不足。我们用数学越狱模型形式化这一现象，描述有效文本模糊化的微妙边界，并分析观察到的越狱行为。在该模型的指导下，我们提出了巴别尔，一个高效的黑箱攻击框架，通过系统的模糊采样和迭代反馈驱动的分布优化，利用识别出的安全漏洞，实现可靠且高成功率的越狱攻击，而无需访问模型内部。对前沿商业模型的全面评估表明，巴别尔实现了最先进的攻击成功率和优越的查询效率。具体而言，与最先进的方法相比，巴别尔在GPT-4o上的攻击成功率从41.33%提高到82.67%，在Claude-3-5-haiku上的攻击成功率从38.33%提高到78.33%，平均查询次数为40，为LLMs安全研究提供了强有力的红队方法论。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the vulnerability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks despite safety alignment efforts. IndicSafe: A Benchmark for Evaluating Multilingual LLM Safety in South Asia
Authors: Priyaranjan Pattnayak, Sanchari Chowdhuri
First: 2026-03-18T16:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T17:06:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) are deployed in multilingual settings, their safety behavior in culturally diverse, low-resource languages remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic evaluation of LLM safety across 12 Indic languages, spoken by over 1.2 billion people but underrepresented in LLM training data. Using a dataset of 6,000 culturally grounded prompts spanning caste, religion, gender, health, and politics, we assess 10 leading LLMs on translated variants of the prompt. Our analysis reveals significant safety drift: cross-language agreement is just 12.8\%, and \texttt{SAFE} rate variance exceeds 17\% across languages. Some models over-refuse benign prompts in low-resource scripts, overflag politically sensitive topics, while others fail to flag unsafe generations. We quantify these failures using prompt-level entropy, category bias scores, and multilingual consistency indices. Our findings highlight critical safety generalization gaps in multilingual LLMs and show that safety alignment does not transfer evenly across languages. We release \textsc{IndicSafe}, the first benchmark to enable culturally informed safety evaluation for Indic deployments, and advocate for language-aware alignment strategies grounded in regional harms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IndicSafe：评估南亚多语言LLM安全性的基准
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在多语言环境中的部署，它们在文化多样性和资源匮乏语言中的安全行为仍然不够了解。我们首次系统性地评估了12种印地语言的LLM安全性，这些语言由超过12亿人使用，但在LLM训练数据中代表性不足。使用一个包含6000个与文化相关的提示的数据集，涵盖种姓、宗教、性别、健康和政治，我们评估了10个领先的LLM在提示翻译变体上的表现。 我们的分析揭示了显著的安全漂移：跨语言一致性仅为12.8%，而安全率方差在不同语言间超过17%。一些模型在资源匮乏的脚本中过度拒绝良性提示，过度标记政治敏感话题，而其他模型则未能标记不安全的生成。我们使用提示级熵、类别偏差分数和多语言一致性指数量化这些失败。 我们的发现突显了多语言LLM中关键的安全泛化差距，并表明安全对齐在不同语言间并不均匀转移。我们发布了IndicSafe，这是第一个基准，旨在为印地语言的文化知情安全评估提供支持，并倡导基于区域危害的语言意识对齐策略。

The findings underscore the need for culturally informed safety evaluations and advocate for language-aware alignment strategies, contributing valuable insights for improving LLM deployment in South Asia.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在文化多样性和资源匮乏的语言环境中的安全性行为，特别是在南亚的12种印地语中，这些语言的使用者超过12亿。以往的方法缺乏系统评估，未能考虑这些语言独特的文化背景，导致安全性漂移和跨语言表现不一致。提出的IndicSafe方法通过使用6000个文化相关提示的数据集系统评估LLM的安全性，揭示了仅有12.8%的跨语言一致性和超过17%的安全率差异。本文的贡献在于建立了第一个文化信息安全评估基准，并倡导基于语言的对齐策略。该方法涉及对10种领先LLM在翻译提示上的评估，突显了安全性泛化的关键差距，并展示了在多语言环境中改善安全性对齐的必要性。
Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders for LLM Safety Steering
Authors: Jehyeok Yeon, Federico Cinus, Yifan Wu, Luca Luceri
First: 2025-12-07T04:46:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T09:56:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are increasingly used to extract activation directions for inference-time steering, but their standard sparsity objective treats latent features as independent. This prior can be poorly matched to high-level safety behaviors, where refusal and harmful compliance appear to depend on distributed structure in activation space. We introduce Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders (GSAE), a dictionary-learning method that learns safety-steering directions by smoothing SAE decoder vectors over a neuron co-activation graph and applying the resulting direction bank through a two-gate runtime controller. Empirically, GSAE improves selective refusal across JailbreakBench, HarmBench, and XSTest, increasing harmful-request refusal while keeping benign-prompt refusals low. On Llama-3-8B, replacing the standard SAE with GSAE in an otherwise identical pipeline improves $Δ_s$ by $20.1$ points on JailbreakBench and $16.8$ points on HarmBench. GSAE outperforms activation-steering baselines and black-box guardrails, preserves benign-task performance, generalizes across Llama-3, Mistral, Qwen 2.5, and Phi-4, and remains strong under black-box and gray-box jailbreak attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：图正则化稀疏自编码器用于大型语言模型安全引导
稀疏自编码器（SAE）越来越多地用于提取推理时引导的激活方向，但其标准稀疏性目标将潜在特征视为独立。这一先验可能与高层次的安全行为不匹配，其中拒绝和有害的顺从似乎依赖于激活空间中的分布结构。我们引入图正则化稀疏自编码器（GSAE），这是一种字典学习方法，通过在神经元共同激活图上平滑SAE解码器向量来学习安全引导方向，并通过双门运行时控制器应用结果方向库。实证结果表明，GSAE在JailbreakBench、HarmBench和XSTest上改善了选择性拒绝，增加了有害请求的拒绝，同时保持良性提示的拒绝率较低。在Llama-3-8B上，在其他条件相同的管道中用GSAE替换标准SAE，使得JailbreakBench的$Δ_s$提高了$20.1$点，HarmBench提高了$16.8$点。GSAE优于激活引导基线和黑箱护栏，保持良性任务性能，在Llama-3、Mistral、Qwen 2.5和Phi-4上具有良好的泛化能力，并在黑箱和灰箱越狱攻击下表现强劲。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of standard sparse autoencoders (SAEs) in extracting activation directions for safety steering in large language models (LLMs), where the independence assumption of latent features does not align well with the complex nature of safety behaviors. Previous methods have struggled with this issue, leading to inadequate performance in distinguishing between harmful and benign requests. The proposed Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders (GSAE) enhance the learning process by incorporating a neuron co-activation graph to smooth decoder vectors, thus providing a more structured approach to safety steering. This method is well-motivated as it directly targets the distributed nature of safety behaviors. The contribution of the paper is significant, demonstrating that GSAE improves selective refusal rates on various benchmarks, achieving a 20.1-point increase on JailbreakBench and a 16.8-point increase on HarmBench while maintaining performance on benign tasks and generalizing across multiple LLMs, effectively supporting the research goals.
本研究解决了标准稀疏自编码器（SAE）在大型语言模型（LLM）安全引导中的局限性，标准稀疏目标假设潜在特征独立，未能捕捉安全行为的分布特性。以往方法未能有效处理激活空间的复杂性，导致拒绝和合规任务的性能不佳。提出的图正则化稀疏自编码器（GSAE）通过结合神经元共激活图来平滑解码器向量，从而增强安全引导方向的学习，提高模型拒绝有害请求的能力，同时保持对良性响应的反应。该方法在选择性拒绝指标上表现出显著改善，在Llama-3-8B上，JailbreakBench提高了20.1分，HarmBench提高了16.8分，超越了现有的激活引导方法，并在攻击场景下保持了跨多种模型的性能。
Benchmark of Benchmarks: Unpacking Influence and Code Repository Quality in LLM Safety Benchmarks
Authors: Junjie Chu, Xinyue Shen, Ye Leng, Michael Backes, Yun Shen, Yang Zhang
First: 2026-03-03T09:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T18:30:07+00:00
Comments: 24 pages. 19 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid expansion of research in LLM safety presents challenges in tracking advancements, making benchmarks important evaluation infrastructures for identifying key trends and facilitating systematic comparisons. Yet no systematic assessment exists of their code quality and runnability, nor of what factors are associated with the community's adoption of certain benchmarks over others. To address this gap, we conduct a systematic measurement study of 31 LLM safety benchmarks (covering prompt injection, jailbreak, and hallucination) with 382 non-benchmark papers as a control group, combining automated static analysis, human runnability testing (220+ person-hours), and bibliometric analysis. We find that only 39\% of benchmark repositories can run without modification, only 16\% provide flawless installation guides, and a mere 6\% include ethical considerations despite containing potentially harmful content. These deficiencies persist across the study period with no significant improvement. Analyzing adoption factors, we find that benchmark adoption correlates with author prominence and code runnability, but not with code quality standards such as Pylint score and maintainability, suggesting that the community's benchmark selection does not reward higher coding standards. Based on these results, we identify potential safety and reliability concerns. Some safety benchmark repositories openly expose harmful content, such as successful jailbreak responses, without any ethical warning or access control, effectively serving as unguarded attack resources. Furthermore, when benchmarks require ad-hoc modifications to run, downstream safety evaluations across different papers may not be comparable. We present case studies illustrating these concrete consequences and propose a targeted checklist to help benchmark contributors improve code quality, documentation, and ethical practices.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基准中的基准：解读LLM安全基准中的影响力和代码库质量
LLM安全研究的快速扩展带来了跟踪进展的挑战，使得基准成为识别关键趋势和促进系统比较的重要评估基础设施。然而，目前尚无对其代码质量和可运行性的系统评估，也没有研究社区对某些基准的采用与其他基准之间的关联因素。为了解决这一空白，我们对31个LLM安全基准（涵盖提示注入、越狱和幻觉）进行系统测量研究，并以382篇非基准论文作为对照组，结合自动静态分析、人为可运行性测试（220+人小时）和文献计量分析。我们发现，只有39%的基准代码库可以在不修改的情况下运行，只有16%提供无瑕疵的安装指南，尽管包含潜在有害内容，仅有6%考虑了伦理问题。这些缺陷在研究期间持续存在，没有显著改善。在分析采用因素时，我们发现基准采用与作者知名度和代码可运行性相关，但与代码质量标准（如Pylint评分和可维护性）无关，这表明社区的基准选择并未奖励更高的编码标准。基于这些结果，我们识别出潜在的安全和可靠性问题。一些安全基准代码库公开暴露有害内容，例如成功的越狱响应，而没有任何伦理警告或访问控制，实际上充当了无防护的攻击资源。此外，当基准需要临时修改才能运行时，不同论文之间的下游安全评估可能无法比较。我们展示了这些具体后果的案例研究，并提出了一份针对性的检查清单，以帮助基准贡献者提高代码质量、文档和伦理实践。

Previous methods did not adequately evaluate these aspects, leading to issues such as low runnability and poor documentation, which the proposed approach seeks to rectify through a comprehensive measurement study of 31 LLM safety benchmarks and a control group of 382 non-benchmark papers. This study combines automated static analysis, human testing, and bibliometric analysis to reveal significant deficiencies in benchmark repositories, including low runnability and ethical considerations. The findings indicate that benchmark adoption is influenced more by author prominence than by code quality, raising safety and reliability concerns. The Great Pretender: A Stochasticity Problem in LLM Jailbreak
Authors: Jean-Philippe Monteuuis, Cong Chen, Jonathan Petit
First: 2026-05-14T06:05:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T06:05:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
"Oh-Oh, yes, I'm the great pretender. Pretending that I'm doing well. My need is such, I pretend too much..." summarizes the state in the area of jailbreak creation and evaluation. You find this method to generate adversarial attacks proposed by a reputable institution (e.g., BoN from Anthropic or Crescendo from Microsoft Research). However, this method does not deliver on the promise claimed in the paper despite having top ASR scores against industry-grade LLMs. You successfully generate the jailbreak prompts against your target (open) model. However, the generated jailbreak prompt works against the target model with a 50% consecutive success rate (5 out of 10 attempts) despite having an 80% ASR (on paper) on the latest closed-source model (with a guardrail system)! This observation leads us to think. First, Attack Success Rate (ASR), the primary metric for LLM jailbreak benchmarking, is not a stable quantity. Second, published ASR numbers are therefore systematically inflated and incomparable across papers. Therefore, we wonder "Why a successful jailbreak prompt does not perform consistently well against a target model on which the prompts have been optimized?". To answer this question, we study the impact of stochasticity not only during attack evaluation but also during attack generation. Our evaluation includes several jailbreak attacks, models (different sizes and providers), and judges. In addition, we propose a new metric and two new frameworks (CAS-eval and CAS-gen). Our evaluation framework, CAS-eval, shows that an attack can have an ASR drop of up to 30 percentage points when a jailbreak prompt needs to succeed on more than one attempt. Thankfully, our attack generation framework (CAS-gen) improves previous jailbreak methods and helps them recover this loss of 30 percentage points!
中文标题/摘要
标题：伟大的伪装者：LLM越狱中的随机性问题
"哦-哦，是的，我是伟大的伪装者。假装我做得很好。我的需求如此，我假装得太多……"总结了越狱创建和评估领域的现状。你发现了由一个知名机构（例如，Anthropic的BoN或微软研究院的Crescendo）提出的生成对抗攻击的方法。然而，尽管在行业级LLM上具有顶级的ASR分数，这种方法并未兑现论文中所声称的承诺。你成功地针对目标（开放）模型生成了越狱提示。然而，生成的越狱提示在目标模型上的连续成功率为50%（10次尝试中有5次成功），尽管在最新的闭源模型（带有护栏系统）上在纸面上有80%的ASR！这一观察促使我们思考。首先，攻击成功率（ASR），作为LLM越狱基准测试的主要指标，并不是一个稳定的量。其次，发布的ASR数字因此系统性地被夸大，并且在不同论文之间不可比。因此，我们想知道“为什么成功的越狱提示在经过优化的目标模型上表现不一致？”为了回答这个问题，我们研究了随机性在攻击评估和攻击生成中的影响。我们的评估包括几种越狱攻击、模型（不同大小和提供者）和评审。此外，我们提出了一个新指标和两个新框架（CAS-eval和CAS-gen）。我们的评估框架CAS-eval显示，当越狱提示需要在多次尝试中成功时，攻击的ASR可能下降多达30个百分点。值得庆幸的是，我们的攻击生成框架（CAS-gen）改进了之前的越狱方法，并帮助它们恢复这30个百分点的损失！
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inconsistencies in the effectiveness of jailbreak prompts for large language models (LLMs), highlighting that existing methods, such as those from reputable institutions, often report inflated Attack Success Rates (ASR) that do not translate to real-world performance. The proposed approach introduces two frameworks, CAS-eval and CAS-gen, which account for stochasticity in both the evaluation and generation of jailbreak prompts, thus providing a more reliable assessment of their effectiveness. The contribution lies in demonstrating that ASR can significantly drop when prompts are tested across multiple attempts, revealing the unreliability of current metrics. The methodology involves evaluating various jailbreak attacks across different models and sizes, ultimately showing that CAS-gen can recover up to 30 percentage points of ASR loss, thereby enhancing the robustness of jailbreak attempts against target models.
本文探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）监狱突破提示的评估和创建中的挑战，强调现有方法（如来自知名机构的方法）通常报告的攻击成功率（ASR）被夸大，无法反映实际性能。所提出的方法通过引入新的评估框架（CAS-eval）和生成框架（CAS-gen），考虑了评估和生成过程中的随机性，从而有所不同。这一方法的动机源于观察到，尽管现有方法可能实现高ASR分数，但在实际应用中并不总是成功。本文的贡献在于证明，当提示需要多次成功时，ASR可能显著下降，而新的框架有效地缓解了这一问题，在各种模型中生成可靠的监狱突破提示时实现了更好的性能。研究结果表明，所提出的方法可以增强监狱突破尝试的稳定性和可靠性，支持创建更有效的对抗攻击的目标。
Reducing the Safety Tax in LLM Safety Alignment with On-Policy Self-Distillation
Authors: Yu Fu, Longxuan Yu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Zhipeng Wei, Hui Liu, N. Benjamin Erichson, Yue Dong
First: 2026-05-14T03:40:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T03:40:07+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment often improves robustness to harmful queries at the cost of reasoning ability, a tradeoff known as the safety tax. A common cause is distributional mismatch: supervised fine-tuning trains the target model on safety demonstrations produced by humans, external models, or fixed self-generated traces, rather than on trajectories sampled from its own policy. We identify off-policy training mismatch as a second source of this tax and study on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment, which we call OPSA. The model generates its own rollouts and receives dense per-token KL supervision from a frozen teacher copy of itself conditioned on a privileged safety context. Because this teacher must be safer than the sampled student trajectory, we introduce \emph{teacher flip rate}: a criterion that measures how often a privileged context converts unsafe responses into safe ones. We use this signal to search for contexts that activate latent safety reasoning rather than merely elicit safe-looking demonstrations. Across two reasoning-model families and five model scales, OPSA achieves a stronger safety--reasoning tradeoff than off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation under matched data and full-parameter fine-tuning, with the largest gains on smaller models (+8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B). The gains persist across training-set sizes and adaptive jailbreak evaluations. Token-level analyses further show that OPSA concentrates updates near early compliance-decision tokens, providing a mechanism for improving safety while preserving general reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过策略自蒸馏减少大语言模型安全对齐中的安全税
安全对齐通常在提高对有害查询的鲁棒性的同时牺牲推理能力，这种权衡被称为安全税。一个常见原因是分布不匹配：监督微调在由人类、外部模型或固定自生成轨迹产生的安全示范上训练目标模型，而不是在其自身策略采样的轨迹上。我们将离策略训练不匹配识别为这种税的第二个来源，并研究用于安全对齐的策略自蒸馏，称为OPSA。该模型生成自己的回滚，并从一个冻结的教师副本中接收每个标记的密集KL监督，该副本基于特权安全上下文进行条件化。由于这个教师必须比采样的学生轨迹更安全，我们引入了“教师翻转率”：一个衡量特权上下文将不安全响应转化为安全响应的频率的标准。我们使用这个信号来寻找激活潜在安全推理的上下文，而不仅仅是引出看似安全的示范。在两个推理模型系列和五个模型规模中，OPSA在匹配数据和全参数微调下实现了比离策略自蒸馏和外部教师蒸馏更强的安全-推理权衡，在较小模型上获得了最大的提升（R1-Distill-1.5B上提高8.85分，Qwen3-0.6B上提高5.49分）。这些提升在训练集大小和自适应越狱评估中持续存在。标记级分析进一步表明，OPSA将更新集中在早期合规决策标记附近，提供了一种在保持一般推理的同时提高安全性的机制。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the challenge of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), which often leads to a tradeoff known as the safety tax, where enhancing safety reduces reasoning ability. Previous methods, such as off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation, suffer from distributional mismatch and do not effectively leverage the model's own policy for safety training. The proposed approach, on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment (OPSA), mitigates these issues by allowing the model to generate its own rollouts and receive supervision from a safer teacher model, thus improving the safety-reasoning balance. The contribution of this paper lies in demonstrating that OPSA achieves superior performance compared to existing methods, particularly on smaller models, with significant improvements in safety and reasoning tradeoffs across various model scales and training conditions. The methodology involves using a teacher flip rate to identify contexts that enhance safety reasoning, resulting in notable performance gains, such as +8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B, while maintaining general reasoning capabilities.
本研究解决了大型语言模型（LLMs）中的安全对齐挑战，这通常导致所谓的安全税权衡，即增强对有害查询的鲁棒性会削弱推理能力。以往的方法，如离线自蒸馏和外部教师蒸馏，存在分布不匹配的问题，未能充分利用模型自身策略进行训练，导致安全性和推理性能不理想。所提出的方法，即用于安全对齐的在线自蒸馏（OPSA），通过允许模型生成自己的回滚并从冻结的教师模型接收监督来缓解这些问题，从而确保训练上下文促进更安全的响应。本文贡献了一种新颖的方法论，有效平衡安全性和推理，证明OPSA在不同模型系列和规模上实现了安全与推理权衡的显著改善，尤其在较小模型上表现出显著的性能提升，从而支持了在不妨碍推理能力的情况下增强LLM安全性的目标。
Quantifying LLM Safety Degradation Under Repeated Attacks Using Survival Analysis
Authors: Zvi Topol
First: 2026-05-13T01:26:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T01:26:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in a wide range of applications, yet remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that circumvent their safety guardrails. Existing evaluation frameworks typically report binary success/failure metrics, failing to capture the temporal dynamics of how attacks succeed under persistent adversarial pressure. This preliminary work proposes a novel evaluation framework that applies survival analysis techniques to characterize LLM jailbreak vuln`erability. Our approach models the time-to-jailbreak as a survival outcome, enabling estimation of hazard functions, survival curves, and risk factors associated with successful attacks. We evaluate three LLMs against a subset of prompts from the HarmBench dataset spanning three attack categories. Our analysis reveals that models exhibit distinct vulnerability profiles: while one model demonstrates rapid degradation under iterative attacks, the two other models show consistent moderate vulnerability. Our framework provides actionable insights for model and LLM application developers and establishes survival analysis as a rigorous methodology for LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用生存分析量化重复攻击下的LLM安全性下降
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越广泛地应用于各种场景，但仍然容易受到绕过安全防护的对抗性越狱攻击。现有评估框架通常报告二元成功/失败指标，未能捕捉在持续对抗压力下攻击成功的时间动态。本初步工作提出了一种新颖的评估框架，应用生存分析技术来表征LLM越狱脆弱性。我们的方法将越狱时间建模为生存结果，使得能够估计危险函数、生存曲线和与成功攻击相关的风险因素。我们对三种LLM进行了评估，使用了来自HarmBench数据集的三类攻击的部分提示。我们的分析揭示了模型表现出不同的脆弱性特征：虽然一种模型在迭代攻击下迅速下降，另外两种模型则表现出一致的中等脆弱性。我们的框架为模型和LLM应用开发者提供了可操作的见解，并确立了生存分析作为LLM安全评估的严格方法论。

RACC: Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria for LLM Safety Testing
Authors: Zeming Wei, Zhixin Zhang, Chengcan Wu, Yihao Zhang, Xiaokun Luan, Meng Sun
First: 2026-02-02T16:20:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:47:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) face severe safety risks from jailbreak attacks, yet current safety testing largely relies on static datasets and lacks systematic criteria to evaluate test suite quality and adequacy. While coverage criteria have proven effective for smaller neural networks, they are impractical for LLMs due to computational overhead and the entanglement of safety-critical signals with irrelevant neuron activations. To address these issues, we propose RACC (Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria), a set of coverage criteria specialized for LLM safety testing. RACC first extracts safety representations from the LLM's hidden states using a small calibration set of harmful prompts, then measures test prompts' concept activations against these directions, and finally computes coverage through six criteria assessing both individual and compositional safety concept coverage. Experiments on multiple LLMs and safety benchmarks show that RACC reliably rewards high-quality jailbreak test suites while remaining insensitive to redundant or invalid inputs, which is a key distinction that neuron-level criteria fail to make. We further demonstrate RACC's practical value in two applications, including test suite prioritization and attack prompt sampling, and validate its generalization across diverse settings and configurations. Overall, RACC provides a scalable and principled foundation for coverage-guided LLM safety testing.

标题：RACC：面向表示的LLM安全测试覆盖标准
大型语言模型（LLM）面临来自越狱攻击的严重安全风险，但当前的安全测试主要依赖静态数据集，缺乏系统性标准来评估测试套件的质量和充分性。虽然覆盖标准在较小的神经网络中已被证明有效，但由于计算开销和安全关键信号与无关神经元激活的纠缠，它们在LLM中不切实际。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了RACC（面向表示的覆盖标准），这是一组专门针对LLM安全测试的覆盖标准。RACC首先使用一小组有害提示从LLM的隐藏状态中提取安全表示，然后根据这些方向测量测试提示的概念激活，最后通过六个标准计算覆盖，评估个体和组合安全概念的覆盖。对多个LLM和安全基准的实验表明，RACC可靠地奖励高质量的越狱测试套件，同时对冗余或无效输入保持不敏感，这是神经元级标准无法做到的关键区别。我们进一步展示了RACC在两个应用中的实际价值，包括测试套件优先级排序和攻击提示采样，并验证了其在不同设置和配置中的泛化能力。总体而言，RACC为覆盖引导的LLM安全测试提供了可扩展和原则性的基础。

FragBench: Cross-Session Attacks Hidden in Benign-Looking Fragments
Authors: Astha Mehta, Niruthiha Selvanayagam, Cedric Lam, Hengxu Li, Phuc-Nguyen Nguyen, Raymond Lee, Olivia McGoffin, My, Luong, Arthur Collé, Jamie Johnson, David Williams-King, Linh Le
First: 2026-05-10T21:06:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T21:06:48+00:00
Comments: preprint of submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
An attacker can split a malicious goal into sub-prompts that each look benign on their own and only become harmful in combination. Existing LLM safety benchmarks evaluate prompts one at a time, or across turns of a single chat, and so do not look for a malicious signal spread across separate sessions with no shared context. We build FragBench, a benchmark drawn from 24 real-world cyber-incident campaigns, which keeps the full attack trail: the multi-fragment kill chain, the per-fragment safety-judge verdicts, sandboxed execution traces, and a matched set of benign cover sessions. FragBench splits this trail into two paired tasks: an adversarial rewriter that hardens fragments against a single-turn safety judge (FragBench Attack), and a graph-based user-level detector trained on the resulting interactions (FragBench Defense). The single-turn judge is near chance on the released corpus by construction, but four GNN variants and three classical-ML baselines all recover the cross-session feature, reaching aggregate event-level F1 = 0.88-0.96. Defending against fragmented LLM misuse therefore requires modeling the cross-session interaction graph, rather than isolated prompts. Our generator, rewriter, sandbox harness, and detector are released at https://github.com/LidaSafety/fragbench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FragBench：隐藏在看似良性片段中的跨会话攻击
攻击者可以将恶意目标拆分为看似良性的子提示，这些子提示单独看时无害，但组合在一起时会变得有害。现有的LLM安全基准一次评估一个提示，或在单个聊天的多个回合中评估，因此未能寻找跨会话的恶意信号，这些会话之间没有共享上下文。我们构建了FragBench，这是一个基于24个真实网络事件活动的基准，保留了完整的攻击轨迹：多片段杀伤链、每个片段的安全评判结果、沙箱执行痕迹，以及一组匹配的良性覆盖会话。FragBench将这一轨迹分为两个配对任务：一个对抗重写器，旨在增强片段对单回合安全评判的抵抗力（FragBench Attack），以及一个基于图的用户级检测器，训练于结果交互（FragBench Defense）。单回合评判在发布的语料库中几乎是随机的，但四种GNN变体和三种经典机器学习基线都恢复了跨会话特征，达到聚合事件级F1 = 0.88-0.96。因此，防御碎片化的LLM误用需要建模跨会话交互图，而不是孤立的提示。我们的生成器、重写器、沙箱工具和检测器已在https://github.com/LidaSafety/fragbench发布。

Theoretical Limits of Language Model Alignment
Authors: Lucas Monteiro Paes, Natalie Mackraz, Barry-John Theobald, Federico Danieli
First: 2026-05-08T01:32:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-08T01:32:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Language model (LM) alignment improves model outputs to reflect human preferences while preserving the capabilities of the base model. The most common alignment approaches are (i) reinforcement learning, which maximizes the expected reward under a KL-divergence constraint, and (ii) best-of-$N$ alignment, which selects the highest-reward output among $N$ independent samples. Despite their widespread use, the fundamental limits of reward improvement under a KL budget remain poorly understood. We characterize the information-theoretic limits of KL-regularized alignment by deriving the maximum achievable expected reward gain for a fixed KL-divergence budget. Our first result provides a closed-form expression for the optimal reward improvement, governed by a Jeffreys divergence term rather than the $\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$ used in prior analyses. We further reformulate this expression as a covariance under the base model, yielding a practical estimator that predicts achievable alignment gains from base model samples alone. We extend our analysis to the proxy reward setting, showing that the gap between ideal and proxy alignment (reward hacking) grows with the magnitude of reward error and when the KL penalty factor decreases. We then prove that reward ensembling mitigates reward hacking, providing a theoretical justification for this technique used in practice. Empirically, we compute the KL-reward Pareto frontier for two tasks for LMs, safety and summarization, and show that best-of-$N$ closely approaches the theoretical limit, while PPO and GRPO remain substantially suboptimal. Our theoretical results shed light on several empirically observed phenomena in the alignment literature and suggest that algorithmic improvements are needed to achieve optimal alignment without high inference costs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语言模型对齐的理论极限
语言模型（LM）对齐改善模型输出，使其反映人类偏好，同时保留基础模型的能力。最常见的对齐方法是（i）强化学习，在KL散度约束下最大化期望奖励，以及（ii）最佳中的$N$对齐，从$N$个独立样本中选择最高奖励输出。尽管这些方法被广泛使用，但在KL预算下奖励改善的基本极限仍然不甚了解。我们通过推导固定KL散度预算下可实现的最大期望奖励增益，来表征KL正则化对齐的信息论极限。我们的第一个结果提供了最优奖励改善的封闭形式表达式，该表达式由Jeffreys散度项主导，而不是先前分析中使用的$\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$。我们进一步将该表达式重新表述为基础模型下的协方差，得出一个实用的估计器，仅通过基础模型样本预测可实现的对齐增益。我们将分析扩展到代理奖励设置，表明理想对齐与代理对齐（奖励黑客）之间的差距随着奖励误差的大小和KL惩罚因子的降低而增加。然后我们证明奖励集成可以减轻奖励黑客，为这一实践中使用的技术提供理论依据。通过实证，我们计算了两个任务（安全性和摘要）的KL-奖励帕累托前沿，并显示最佳中的$N$接近理论极限，而PPO和GRPO仍然显著次优。我们的理论结果阐明了对齐文献中观察到的若干经验现象，并建议需要算法改进以在不高推理成本的情况下实现最优对齐。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the theoretical limits of language model alignment, which aims to enhance model outputs to better reflect human preferences while maintaining the model's capabilities. Previous methods, such as reinforcement learning and best-of-$N$ alignment, have been widely used but suffer from a lack of understanding regarding the fundamental limits of reward improvement under a KL-divergence budget. The proposed approach characterizes these limits by deriving a closed-form expression for optimal reward improvement, governed by Jeffreys divergence, and reformulates it to yield a practical estimator for predicting alignment gains. The contribution of this research lies in its theoretical insights into alignment techniques and the demonstration that reward ensembling can mitigate reward hacking. Empirical results show that best-of-$N$ alignment approaches the theoretical limit in tasks like safety and summarization, while traditional methods like PPO and GRPO are significantly less effective, indicating the need for algorithmic improvements to achieve optimal alignment efficiently.
本文探讨了现有语言模型（LM）对齐方法的局限性，特别是强化学习和最佳$N$对齐，这些方法在KL散度约束下难以最大化奖励提升。提出的方法表征了KL正则化对齐的信息论极限，推导出由Jeffreys散度主导的最优奖励提升的封闭形式表达，而不是之前使用的$\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$。该方法提供了一种基于基础模型样本预测对齐增益的实用估计器，并将分析扩展到代理奖励，揭示奖励集成可以缓解奖励黑客问题。研究方法包括对安全性和摘要任务的KL-奖励帕累托前沿的实证评估，表明最佳$N$方法接近理论极限，而其他方法如PPO和GRPO的效果显著低于最佳水平。这些发现突显了在高效实现最佳对齐方面需要算法改进。
When No Benchmark Exists: Validating Comparative LLM Safety Scoring Without Ground-Truth Labels
Authors: Sushant Gautam, Finn Schwall, Annika Willoch Olstad, Fernando Vallecillos Ruiz, Birk Torpmann-Hagen, Sunniva Maria Stordal Bjørklund, Leon Moonen, Klas Pettersen, Michael A. Riegler
First: 2026-05-07T17:56:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T17:56:41+00:00
Comments: SimpleAudit Repository: https://github.com/kelkalot/simpleaudit
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Many deployments must compare candidate language models for safety before a labeled benchmark exists for the relevant language, sector, or regulatory regime. We formalize this setting as benchmarkless comparative safety scoring and specify the contract under which a scenario-based audit can be interpreted as deployment evidence. Scores are valid only under a fixed scenario pack, rubric, auditor, judge, sampling configuration, and rerun budget. Because no labels are available, we replace ground-truth agreement with an instrumental-validity chain: responsiveness to a controlled safe-versus-abliterated contrast, dominance of target-driven variance over auditor and judge artifacts, and stability across reruns. We instantiate the chain in SimpleAudit, a local-first scoring instrument, and validate it on a Norwegian safety pack. Safe and abliterated targets separate with AUROC values between 0.89 and 1.00, target identity is the dominant variance component ($η^2 \approx 0.52$), and severity profiles stabilize by ten reruns. Applying the same chain to Petri shows that it admits both tools. The substantial differences arise upstream of the chain, in claim-contract enforcement and deployment fit. A Norwegian public-sector procurement case comparing Borealis and Gemma 3 demonstrates the resulting evidence in practice: the safer model depends on scenario category and risk measure. Consequently, scores, matched deltas, critical rates, uncertainty, and the auditor and judge used must be reported together rather than collapsed into a single ranking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当没有基准时：在没有真实标签的情况下验证比较LLM安全评分
许多部署必须在相关语言、行业或监管制度的标记基准存在之前比较候选语言模型的安全性。我们将这种情况形式化为无基准的比较安全评分，并指定场景基础审计可以被解释为部署证据的合同。分数仅在固定的场景包、评分标准、审计员、评判者、抽样配置和重跑预算下有效。由于没有可用的标签，我们用工具有效性链替代真实一致性：对受控的安全与消除对比的响应、目标驱动方差对审计员和评判者伪影的主导性，以及重跑的稳定性。我们在SimpleAudit中实例化该链，这是一个本地优先的评分工具，并在挪威安全包上验证。安全和消除目标的AUROC值在0.89到1.00之间，目标身份是主导方差成分（$η^2 \approx 0.52$），严重性轮廓在十次重跑中稳定。将相同的链应用于Petri表明它同时接受这两种工具。显著差异出现在链的上游，在索赔合同执行和部署适配中。一个比较Borealis和Gemma 3的挪威公共部门采购案例展示了实践中的证据：更安全的模型依赖于场景类别和风险度量。因此，分数、匹配的增量、关键率、不确定性以及使用的审计员和评判者必须一起报告，而不是合并为单一排名。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenge of evaluating language model safety in scenarios where no labeled benchmarks exist, which is critical for various deployments. Previous methods rely on ground-truth labels for safety assessments, leading to limitations in their applicability across different contexts. The proposed approach, termed benchmarkless comparative safety scoring, introduces a framework that utilizes scenario-based audits and an instrumental-validity chain to validate safety scores without requiring ground-truth labels. This method is well-motivated as it allows for the assessment of language models in diverse regulatory environments. The paper contributes by presenting SimpleAudit, a scoring instrument that was validated using a Norwegian safety pack, achieving AUROC values between 0.89 and 1.00, indicating effective differentiation between safe and abliterated targets. The findings demonstrate that the proposed methodology can reliably support safety evaluations in the absence of traditional benchmarks.
本研究解决了在缺乏标注基准的情况下评估语言模型安全性的问题，这对于各个领域的部署至关重要。以往的方法依赖于安全评估的真实标签，这在没有这些标签的情况下存在局限性。所提出的方法引入了无基准比较安全评分，利用基于场景的审计框架，强调工具有效性链，以确保在没有真实标签的情况下进行可靠评估。该方法在名为SimpleAudit的工具中实现，并使用挪威安全包进行了验证，成功区分安全和消除目标的AUROC值在0.89到1.00之间。研究结果表明，所提出的方法有效解决了现有方法的局限性，通过提供一种结构化的方式来评估模型安全性，展示了安全评分可能因场景和风险度量而显著变化，从而为实际模型比较提供了有价值的见解。
Beyond Accuracy: Policy Invariance as a Reliability Test for LLM Safety Judges
Authors: Shihao Weng, Yang Feng, Xiaofei Xie
First: 2026-05-07T12:49:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:49:09+00:00
Comments: 9 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM-as-a-Judge pipelines have become the de facto evaluator for agent safety, yet existing benchmarks treat their verdicts as ground-truth proxies without checking whether the verdicts depend on the agent's behavior or merely on how the evaluation policy happens to be worded. We argue that any trustworthy safety judge must satisfy a basic property we call policy invariance, and we operationalize it as three testable principles: rubric-semantics invariance under certified-equivalent rewrites, rubric-threshold invariance under intentional strict-to-lenient shifts, and ambiguity-aware calibration so that verdict instability concentrates on genuinely ambiguous cases. Instantiating these principles as a stress-test protocol with four agent-class judges on trajectories drawn from ASSEBench and R-Judge, we surface a previously unmeasured failure mode: today's judges respond to meaningful normative shifts and to meaningless structural rewrites with comparable strength, and cannot tell the two apart. Content-preserving policy rewrites flip up to 9.1% of verdicts above baseline jitter, and 18-43% of all observed flips occur on unambiguous cases under such rewrites, so existing safety scores conflate what the agent did with how the evaluator was prompted. Beyond the diagnosis, we contribute the Policy Invariance Score and the Judge Card reporting protocol, which expose an order-of-magnitude spread in judge reliability that is invisible to accuracy-only leaderboards. We release the protocol and code so that future agent-safety benchmarks can audit their own evaluators rather than trust them by default.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越准确性：政策不变性作为LLM安全评判的可靠性测试
LLM作为评判的管道已成为代理安全的事实评估者，但现有基准将其裁决视为真实代理，而未检查裁决是否依赖于代理的行为或仅仅取决于评估政策的措辞。我们认为，任何值得信赖的安全评判必须满足我们称之为政策不变性的基本属性，并将其操作化为三个可测试的原则：在经过认证的等效重写下的评分语义不变性、在有意的严格到宽松的转变下的评分阈值不变性，以及意识到模糊性的校准，以便裁决的不稳定性集中在真正模糊的案例上。将这些原则实例化为一个压力测试协议，使用来自ASSEBench和R-Judge的轨迹上的四个代理类别评判，我们揭示了一种以前未测量的失败模式：今天的评判对有意义的规范性变化和无意义的结构重写的反应强度相当，且无法区分二者。内容保持的政策重写使得高达9.1%的裁决在基线抖动之上翻转，且在此类重写下，18-43%的所有观察到的翻转发生在明确的案例上，因此现有的安全评分混淆了代理的行为与评估者的提示方式。除了诊断，我们贡献了政策不变性评分和评判卡报告协议，揭示了评判可靠性在仅依赖准确性排行榜上不可见的数量级差异。我们发布了该协议和代码，以便未来的代理安全基准可以审计自己的评估者，而不是默认信任他们。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of current LLM-as-a-Judge pipelines, which evaluate agent safety but often treat their verdicts as definitive without assessing their dependence on the evaluation policy's wording. Previous methods failed to ensure that judges' decisions were consistent across different contexts, leading to unreliable safety assessments. The proposed approach introduces the concept of policy invariance, operationalized through three testable principles that enhance the reliability of safety judgments. This methodology includes a stress-test protocol applied to four agent-class judges using data from ASSEBench and R-Judge, revealing that existing judges struggle to differentiate between meaningful and meaningless shifts in evaluation criteria. The paper contributes the Policy Invariance Score and the Judge Card reporting protocol, highlighting significant discrepancies in judge reliability that are not captured by traditional accuracy metrics, thus providing a more robust framework for evaluating agent safety.
本文探讨了用于评估代理安全性的LLM作为评判者管道的可靠性，强调现有基准往往将评判者的裁决视为准确，而未评估其对评估政策措辞的依赖性。以往的方法未能确保安全评判者在不同上下文中保持一致的裁决，可能导致对代理行为的误解。所提出的方法引入了政策不变性的概念，通过三个可测试的原则进行操作，作为评估评判者可靠性的压力测试协议。研究方法涉及将这些原则应用于四个代理类别的评判者，使用来自ASSEBench和R-Judge的轨迹，揭示了一个显著的失败模式，即评判者无法区分评估标准中的有意义和无意义的变化。研究结果表明，现有的安全评分可能将代理行为与评估者提示混淆，导致不可靠的评估。本文贡献了政策不变性评分和评判者卡报告协议，以增强评判者可靠性的评估，超越单纯的准确性指标。
XL-SafetyBench: A Country-Grounded Cross-Cultural Benchmark for LLM Safety and Cultural Sensitivity
Authors: Dasol Choi, Eugenia Kim, Jaewon Noh, Sang Seo, Eunmi Kim, Myunggyo Oh, Yunjin Park, Brigitta Jesica Kartono, Josef Pichlmeier, Helena Berndt, Sai Krishna Mendu, Glenn Johannes Tungka, Özlem Gökçe, Suresh Gehlot, Katherine Pratt, Amanda Minnich, Haon Park
First: 2026-05-07T04:35:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T04:35:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current LLM safety benchmarks are predominantly English-centric and often rely on translation, failing to capture country-specific harms. Moreover, they rarely evaluate a model's ability to detect culturally embedded sensitivities as distinct from universal harms. We introduce XL-SafetyBench. a suite of 5,500 test cases across 10 country-language pairs, comprising a Jailbreak Benchmark of country-grounded adversarial prompts and a Cultural Benchmark where local sensitivities are embedded within innocuous requests. Each item is constructed via a multi-stage pipeline that combines LLM-assisted discovery, automated validation gates, and dual independent native-speaker annotators per country. To distinguish principled refusal from comprehension failure, we evaluate Attack Success Rate (ASR) alongside two complementary metrics we introduce: Neutral-Safe Rate (NSR) and Cultural Sensitivity Rate (CSR). Evaluating 10 frontier and 27 local LLMs reveals two key findings. First, jailbreak robustness and cultural awareness do not show a coupled relationship among frontier models, so a composite safety score obscures per-axis variation. Second, local models exhibit a near-linear ASR-NSR trade-off (r = -0.81), indicating that their apparent safety reflects generation failure rather than genuine alignment. XL-SafetyBench enables more nuanced, cross-cultural safety evaluation in the multilingual era.
中文标题/摘要

当前的大型语言模型安全基准主要以英语为中心，通常依赖翻译，未能捕捉特定国家的危害。此外，它们很少评估模型检测文化嵌入敏感性与普遍危害的能力。我们推出了XL-SafetyBench，一个包含5500个测试案例的套件，涵盖10个国家-语言对，包括一个基于国家的对抗性提示的越狱基准和一个将地方敏感性嵌入无害请求中的文化基准。每个项目通过一个多阶段流程构建，该流程结合了大型语言模型辅助发现、自动验证门和每个国家的双独立母语者注释。为了区分原则性拒绝与理解失败，我们评估攻击成功率（ASR）以及我们引入的两个互补指标：中性安全率（NSR）和文化敏感性率（CSR）。对10个前沿和27个地方大型语言模型的评估揭示了两个关键发现。首先，越狱鲁棒性与文化意识在前沿模型中并不呈现耦合关系，因此复合安全评分掩盖了每个轴的变化。其次，地方模型表现出近线性的ASR-NSR权衡（r = -0.81），表明它们的表面安全反映的是生成失败而非真正的对齐。XL-SafetyBench使得在多语言时代进行更细致的跨文化安全评估成为可能。

Safety and accuracy follow different scaling laws in clinical large language models
Authors: Sebastian Wind, Tri-Thien Nguyen, Jeta Sopa, Mahshad Lotfinia, Sebastian Bickelhaup, Michael Uder, Harald Köstler, Gerhard Wellein, Sven Nebelung, Daniel Truhn, Andreas Maier, Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh
First: 2026-05-05T17:57:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T17:57:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Clinical LLMs are often scaled by increasing model size, context length, retrieval complexity, or inference-time compute, with the implicit expectation that higher accuracy implies safer behavior. This assumption is incomplete in medicine, where a few confident, high-risk, or evidence-contradicting errors can matter more than average benchmark performance. We introduce SaFE-Scale, a framework for measuring how clinical LLM safety changes across model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute. To instantiate this framework, we introduce RadSaFE-200, a Radiology Safety-Focused Evaluation benchmark of 200 multiple-choice questions with clinician-defined clean evidence, conflict evidence, and option-level labels for high-risk error, unsafe answer, and evidence contradiction. We evaluated 34 locally deployed LLMs across six deployment conditions: closed-book prompting (zero-shot), clean evidence, conflict evidence, standard RAG, agentic RAG, and max-context prompting. Clean evidence produced the strongest improvement, increasing mean accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1%, while reducing high-risk error from 12.0% to 2.6%, contradiction from 12.7% to 2.3%, and dangerous overconfidence from 8.0% to 1.6%. Standard RAG and agentic RAG did not reproduce this safety profile: agentic RAG improved accuracy over standard RAG and reduced contradiction, but high-risk error and dangerous overconfidence remained elevated. Max-context prompting increased latency without closing the safety gap, and additional inference-time compute produced only limited gains. Worst-case analysis showed that clinically consequential errors concentrated in a small subset of questions. Clinical LLM safety is therefore not a passive consequence of scaling, but a deployment property shaped by evidence quality, retrieval design, context construction, and collective failure behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：临床大型语言模型中的安全性和准确性遵循不同的缩放法则
临床LLM通常通过增加模型大小、上下文长度、检索复杂性或推理时计算来进行缩放，隐含的期望是更高的准确性意味着更安全的行为。这个假设在医学中是不完整的，因为少数自信的高风险或与证据相矛盾的错误可能比平均基准表现更为重要。我们引入了SaFE-Scale，一个测量临床LLM安全性如何随模型规模、证据质量、检索策略、上下文暴露和推理时计算变化的框架。为了实现这个框架，我们引入了RadSaFE-200，一个以放射学安全为重点的评估基准，包含200个多项选择题，具有临床医生定义的干净证据、冲突证据和高风险错误、不安全答案及证据矛盾的选项级标签。我们在六种部署条件下评估了34个本地部署的LLM：闭卷提示（零-shot）、干净证据、冲突证据、标准RAG、代理RAG和最大上下文提示。干净证据产生了最强的改进，将平均准确性从73.5%提高到94.1%，同时将高风险错误从12.0%降低到2.6%，矛盾从12.7%降低到2.3%，危险的过度自信从8.0%降低到1.6%。标准RAG和代理RAG未能重现这一安全特征：代理RAG提高了准确性并减少了矛盾，但高风险错误和危险的过度自信仍然较高。最大上下文提示增加了延迟而未缩小安全差距，额外的推理时计算仅产生有限的收益。最坏情况分析显示，临床相关错误集中在少数问题上。因此，临床LLM的安全性并不是缩放的被动结果，而是由证据质量、检索设计、上下文构建和集体失败行为塑造的部署属性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacy of current scaling methods for clinical large language models (LLMs), which often assume that increased model size and complexity lead to improved safety and accuracy. Previous methods have overlooked the critical impact of high-risk errors in medical contexts, where even a few significant mistakes can have serious consequences. The proposed SaFE-Scale framework offers a novel approach to evaluate clinical LLM safety across various dimensions, including model scale and evidence quality. This study introduces the RadSaFE-200 benchmark, consisting of 200 multiple-choice questions designed to assess safety-focused performance. The evaluation of 34 LLMs revealed that using clean evidence significantly enhanced accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1% while drastically reducing high-risk errors and contradictions. In contrast, other retrieval strategies did not achieve similar safety improvements, indicating that clinical LLM safety is influenced by deployment conditions rather than merely scaling up the models.
